You are an adaptable, analytical and results focused individual with strong reporting and CRM knowledge. You can manage multiple requests and projects with competing deadlines effectively, and love to answer problems with data. You have strong customer service skills in providing information to stakeholders to help solve business needs. 

Primary duties:

Actively build and maintain an inviting company culture.

About the job
Magellan Aerospace has an exciting career opportunity for a full-time permanent Statistical Process Control (SPC) Data Analyst at our manufacturing hub in Winnipeg, Manitoba.

Magellan Aerospace is a global, integrated aerospace company that provides complex assemblies and systems solutions to aircraft and engine manufacturers, and defence and space agencies worldwide. At Magellan we have over 80 years of collective knowledge and experience in the aerospace industry, and believe one truth: People create value.

Employees are our greatest resource in working towards a successful future, and together we build professional relationships that thrive. We know that personal development is fundamental to the success of every individual and invest in our employees by providing excellent career progression opportunities. When you are part of Magellan, you are part of the team!

Position Summary

The SPC Data Analyst will provide technical assistance to Manufacturing Engineering Planning and Operations Management in the implementation of SPC at Magellan Aerospace, Winnipeg. Provide process control training and keep process records. Develop and publish an implementation plan, operation procedure and supporting work instruction for SPC in the Operations Division.

Essential Responsibilities

Provide technical assistance and training as required to support the implementation of Statistical Process Control (SPC) to meet customer and internal requirements. 
Develop and deliver training in SPC. 
Provide technical assistance in the implementation and practice of Statistical Process Control. This includes guidance and support in defining data acquisition methods, tools, hardware, and software and data manipulation to provide appropriate outputs. 
Liaise with internal and external customers as required to support the effective implementation and use of variability reduction to support Customer and Magellan requirements. 
Work with ME/QA department to develop and implement spec plans. 
Research and provide proof of concepts for new inspection technologies and how they can be implemented into MAW processes in order to reduce inspection costs. 
Work with the tool and gauge department to ensure compliance to ISO:17025 requirements for tool calibration, communicate and ship tools to external calibration houses for calibration. 
Review and, where necessary, re-write existing operation procedures and work instructions pertaining to SPC. 
Learn SPC concepts and advanced usage of associated software and hardware. 
Promote and support the utilization of SPC data to improve manufacturing processes. 
Provide analysis and support to utilize SPC data to promote cost savings. 
Identify new technologies and data gathering devices to improve Inspection and SPC process. 
Support metrology department primarily in tracking and analyzing data. 

Position Requirements

Graduate of a recognized Engineering Technologist program or relevant University degree or a minimum of five (5) years related experience in a manufacturing environment. 
Minimum of five (5) years of experience in the application of statistical methods in a manufacturing environment. 
Membership in CTTAM or APEGM if applicable. 
Excellent written and oral communication skills; detail oriented; priority setting; result driven; customer service focused. 

Why Magellan?

Competitive salary
Attractive (FLEX) benefits package (fully Company paid)
Generous Company pension plan
Positive work-life balance
Excellent career progression opportunities
Commitment to professional growth
Company social events including Company BBQ, children's events, service awards day, winter holiday party and many other events put together by our social committee!
Employee Social & Welfare Association
Employee discounts on tickets to certain sporting events and other entertainment/events
On-site parking, gym and cafeteria
Employee Assistance Program (EAP)

Confidentiality

Magellan Aerospace respects the privacy and confidentiality of personal information provided by candidates and shall not disclose to any external parties unless legislated.

Water Security Agency is looking for an enthusiastic individual to join our Informatics unit as an Environmental Business Analyst in our Regina location.

Reporting to the Supervisor, Environmental Business Systems, an employee in this job will provide data management services to support the delivery of Water Security Agency's (WSA) drinking water and wastewater quality vision and the Ministry of Environment’s Environmental Protection Branch’s goals. 

Work is undertaken in a team environment collecting, manipulating, managing and reporting on water quality data as it pertains to drinking water, wastewater, surface water and groundwater. This employee will collaborate with Ministry of Environment to fulfill their solid waste and storage facilities data requirements. The successful candidate will have a Degree in the natural or physical sciences or an equivalent combination of related experience and education and 3 years’ experience with knowledge of general water chemistry, in relation to drinking water, water treatment and wastewater.

About the job
Reports to: National Director, Insights and Performance

Opportunity  
United Way Centraide (UWC) is Canada’s leading network of local community builders empowering people to make lasting social change in their communities. With a presence across Canada, serving over 5000 communities, our network of local United Ways and Centraides tackle the most important social issue of poverty and social exclusion. Our vision is that everyone in every community has the opportunity to reach their full potential. United Way Centraide Canada (UWCC) is the national office that provides leadership and services to UWC members across the country. 

Profile
UWCC data and insight program is an integral part of a broader strategy to position the UWC network for long-term growth and impact.

The data and insights program is a strategic link between operations and business units with a mandate to advance UWCC’s strategic priorities including network wide strategic alignment, interoperability and performance.

Reporting to the National Director of Insights and Performance, the Business Intelligence Analyst will contribute to the development of UWCC’s data insight strategy and maturity roadmap and will support their implementations in the following areas:
Advanced business analytics – Proactive critical analysis of internal and external data sources, their utilization, and identification of opportunities for further insights to support business priorities and decisions.
Empowered self-serve delivery models – Implementation of a “self-serve" principle into existing and new data insight products and services including capacity-building to support change management and enhance adoption.
Data infrastructure, governance, and management - Enhancement of data flow processes, introduction and management of a data governance program.

The successful candidate for this position will have a solid understanding of data analysis, is comfortable working collaboratively in a dynamic and multi-stakeholder environment and has strong curiosity and passion to learn about emerging trends and needs in the community services sectors.

Responsibilities
ADVANCED BUSINESS ANALYTICS 
Work cross-functionally to identify business problems and requirements and collect, clean, manage, and analyze available and related data to advance UWCC’s work using meaningful insights.
Responding to data insight needs, analyze (mine) and interpret internal and secondary data sources, identify trends, patterns, and anomalies, providing insights based on analysis in easy-to-understand formats and reports.
Organizing and presenting data to tell a cohesive story in support of leadership decisions and advancing organizational strategies through prioritizing key data sources, conducting analysis, and identifying key performance indicators.
Provide on-demand analysis for integration into projects across business lines.

EMPOWERED SELF-SERVE DELIVERY MODELS
Ensure business and end users engagement on current state analysis, requirements gathering and backlog prioritization, user acceptance testing, and training on all data insight products.
Design, develop, disseminate, and maintain business intelligence solutions and dashboards to empower teams across the organization with accessible opportunities to explore data, uncover new insights, and take action.
Provide leadership and support in design and execution of training and information sessions within UWCC and across the UWC network on relevant data, insight, and information management practices and products.

DATA INFRASTRUCTURE, GOVERNANCE & MANAGEMENT 
Work with IT and Operations team to improve data management capabilities through data mapping and modelling, identifying data anomalies, ensuring proper data hygiene, and keeping up to date on leading data management practices.

Qualifications
Minimum 3 years’ experience in data analytics and reporting with working knowledge of business intelligence applications.
Post-secondary degree in a relevant field – i.e., Business, Economics, Statistics, Mathematics.
Competent in data analytics techniques – i.e., A/B testing, regression, trend analysis, projections.
Good level of competence with analytics tools such as SPSS, Minitab, R. 
Intermediate understanding of programming languages such as Python, Perl, etc. with the view to processing datasets and automating data analysis, as well as experience with scripting and working with SQL databases.
Advanced knowledge of Excel: data summarizing, statistical functions, optimization.
Solid understanding of data visualization and comfortable working with data visualization tools such as Tableau, PowerBI, Klipfolio. –Programming skills in JavaScript / JQuery/ PHP will be considered an asset.
Solid understanding of business intelligence with strong curiosity and eagerness to develop a deep understanding of the business, learn new skills, and technologies.
Excellent communications skills, enjoys presenting data and complex analyses into stories understood by technical and non-technical stakeholders. 
Strong ability to work with non-technical business partners to gather requirements and plan out data products.
Thrives in teams and can work under dynamic conditions and within deadlines.
Experience working in philanthropy and/or community and social services is an asset.

Location
United Way Centraide’s national office is located in Ottawa, Ontario. The office is an open-space environment and at times, employees work from remote locations. We currently work in a hybrid-remote model. 
 There is a strong preference for the successful candidate to be located in Ottawa but the opportunity is open to individuals across the country.
 Diversity, Equity and Inclusion
 United Way Centraide Canada hires based on merit and is strongly committed to diversity and equity within its community and to providing a welcoming and inclusive workplace. It especially welcomes applications from Black, Indigenous and People of Colour, women, persons with disabilities, people of all sexual orientations and genders, and others with the skills and knowledge to productively engage with diverse communities.

About the job
BC Public School Employers’ Association

Data Analyst
The BC Public School Employers’ Association is looking to hire a Data Analyst to coordinate the collection, analysis, and reporting of information at BCPSEA to support informed decision-making within the K-12 public education system.

Working under the direction of the Manager, Information and Data, the primary responsibility of the Data Analyst position will be to oversee the quarterly collection of human resources information from school districts as part of the Employment Data and Analysis System (EDAS) and prepare reports using this information to inform decision-making by BCPSEA and other stakeholders. The Data Analyst will also support the collection, analysis, and reporting of information for other BCPSEA functional areas on an as-needed basis, including for exempt compensation, finance, and recruitment.

Education and Experience
The Data Analyst must have a college diploma or university degree in data management or a related field and possess strong technical skills, including proficiency with databases (Oracle), data analytics (PowerBI), and spreadsheet software (Excel).

Demonstrated expertise and experience in performing data analysis in a labour relations setting is preferred, as is familiarity with human resources information systems, such as Cayenta, PowerSchool, and PeopleSoft.

Experience in the K-12 public education sector and/or public sector is an asset.

Competitive Compensation and Benefits
The expected starting salary range for this position is $75,602 – $82,273. We offer a competitive benefits package, including extended health, dental and a $2,000 annual Health and Wellness allowance, as well as pension with the Municipal Pension Plan.

Hybrid Structure
BCPSEA is a collegial, hybrid work environment with a combination of optional remote work and in-office work for team-building, training, and as required.

Training
We offer staff regular training and support professional development opportunities. As part of our ongoing commitment to foster a safe and inclusive workplace, all staff will be provided with: Reconciliation; Diversity, Equity, and Inclusion; and Respect in the Workplace training as part of their onboarding with us.

Reconciliation
The BCPSEA office is located at 300 – 2889 East 12th Avenue in Vancouver on the traditional and unceded territory of the xʷməθkʷəy̓ əm (Musqueam), Skwxwú7mesh (Squamish), and səlilwətaɬ (Tsleil-Waututh) peoples. Our work spans across the Province of BC, which is home to thousands of Inuit, Métis, and First Nations peoples across British Columbia, each with unique traditions, history, and culture. We are committed to Reconciliation and to strong Indigenous partnerships and relationships.

Applicants
We invite qualified individuals to apply online on Make a Future at https://bit.ly/4bkl25b with a cover letter and résumé by Friday, March 1, 2024. For questions about this role, please email Chris Beneteau, Executive Director, Employee Relations and Sector Initiatives at chrisb@bcpsea.bc.ca.

- Utilize SQL to query databases, conduct data validation, and perform data transformations to ensure accuracy and reliability of reports.

3. Excel Proficiency:
- Leverage advanced Excel functionalities for data analysis, modeling, and visualization to complement Power BI reporting.

4. Business Analysis and Requirements Gathering:
- Collaborate with stakeholders to understand business needs and gather requirements for reporting and analytics solutions.
- Conduct business analysis to identify opportunities for process improvement and efficiency.

5. Business Decision Support:
- Collaborate with cross-functional teams to understand business requirements and provide data-driven insights to guide decision-making processes.
- Identify opportunities for improvement and efficiency through data analysis, contributing to overall business growth.

6. Experience in Wholesale Distribution:
- Leverage previous experience in a similar business model within the wholesale distribution sector to understand industry-specific challenges and opportunities.

7. Data Governance and Quality:
- Implement and maintain data governance practices to ensure data integrity, accuracy, and security.
- Conduct regular audits to validate the quality of data and recommend improvements as needed.

Want to make a difference in your career?  Consider this opportunity.

The Senior Data Analyst performs a key function in supporting data integrity of identity management services to the healthcare sector on behalf of the Enterprise Data Management portfolio, responsible for the data quality and integrity of data contributed to the provincial EHR data assets. The Senior Data Analyst role is specifically responsible for the data integrity reviews of Admission, Discharge and Transfer (ADT) data contributed to the Provincial Client Registry (PCR / EMPI), as well as reviews of the provider data contributed to the Provincial Provider Registry (PPR).

Here Is What You Will Be Doing

Acts as the primary contact to assigned data sources who contribute to the Patient and Provider Registries (PCR and PPR), such as hospital Health Records Departments and RHPA Colleges, to support data quality and data integrity related error remediation of Personal Information/Personal Health Information (PHI) related records.
Analyzes inbound records against existing records in the PCR and PPR, and manually performs health record set linking, unlinking, and merging functions of records submitted.
Manages relationships with Record Management contacts at the data sources and supports Health or Registration record staff in resolving data integrity related tasks and monitors hospital progress in reducing data integrity task queues.
Provides overviews and training to hospital health record and college department staff, who will be leveraging the PCR and PPR ‘Inspector’ tool, used by data sources for viewing their data integrity tasks and issues.
Works with data sources to further investigate and resolve complex health record overlays and duplicate patient or record situations, where the data source requires additional support for patient unmerges or patient overwrite situations in their own local system, as well as to ensure that the correction is applied in the PCR/PPR.
Supports the onboarding and new data source relationship building to ensure a seamless data quality and integrity process is established, including the regular engagement and follow up with new data sources, to provide assurance of data quality and integrity related record remediation being achieved.
Works with the team to ensure work coverage and tasks are completed as a team effort.
Provides training and mentoring to the Data Analyst I and new hires. 
Maintains responsibility and ownership of assigned tasks, tickets and reports, and ensures the timely completion and conclusion of each until resolution.
Supports other team members in assisting with backlogs or other data quality and integrity initiatives. requiring a senior analyst review and conclusion.
Accountable for service quality for their data source (assigned client), and assurance of data quality and integrity of the data in the PCR/PPR, as these registries are used for supporting the Electronic Health Record overall.
Fosters sustainable, trusted relationships with team members, data sources, and superiors.
Acts as subject matter expert on data source record accuracy.
Identifies and escalates issues, working with the team/colleagues and leadership, as well as external data sources clients to ensure adherence to data quality and integrity standards. 
Builds collaborative relationships with newly onboarded data sources, establishing a reliable and responsive relationship and communication channel for responding to data quality and integrity related requirements.
Makes recommendations based on data integrity and record observations and brings them to Lead/Leadership for review and consideration, supports the implementation of new or enhanced data quality analysis or reporting.
Actively engages in Data Quality and Integrity related activities and reporting and recommends process efficiencies to improve the team function and knowledge. Suggests improvements to increase data quality oversight and reduce the volume of data quality affected records.
Makes key decisions on patient record linking after conducting analysis of the inbound record against existing records. 
Maintains confidentiality and data/system integrity to mitigate privacy incidents or breaches that could result in patient safety concerns.

Education And Experience

Here is what you will need to be successful:

College diploma or Bachelor’s degree in Health Information Management.
Canadian Health Information Management Association (CHIMA) designation is an asset.
3 -5 years of experience working within a Healthcare environment such as a hospital is preferred, or equivalent health care organization or agency.
3- 5 years of health information management experience.
Experience working with personal health information (PHI), and understanding the importance of protection, privacy and security of all records submitted to Ontario Health.
Knowledge of health information management systems.
Knowledge of Legislative boundaries and privacy regulations unique to Ontario and Canada.
Knowledge of Patient safety considerations.

Knowledge And Skills

Ability to compile performance metrics and report summaries.
Ability to identify new data quality and integrity analysis requirements and execute the development and delivery of the process.
Ability to support new data source onboarding and ramp up.
Ability to apply privacy and security expectations on the handling of PHI.
Ability to apply health information management skills and analysis on PHI records.
Ability to apply data analysis skills on the review of patient identity record information.
Ability to apply client relationships skills in managing relationships with key contacts at the data sources (hospitals, colleges, etc.).

Data Governance Analyst (24 months)

Location: Calgary, AB (Hybrid In-Office)

For over 55 years, H&R Block has prepared taxes for millions of Canadians annually. Headquartered in Calgary, Alberta, we serve taxpayers in more than 1,000+ offices, through our upload from home service, and online with our DIY tax software. Becoming an H&R Block Associate is an opportunity to grow with the strongest brand in the tax preparation industry. We know that the ability to deliver outstanding client service starts with having the best talent on our team, and if you want to be part of our success story then we want to hear from you!

The Opportunity:
Under the direction of the Director, Delivery Services & Data Governance, the Data Governance Analyst will join a team responsible for business execution and delivery of solutions to our operating teams. This role will be responsible for implementing an Information Governance roadmap and operating the practice, ensuring the organization’s data is accurate, reliable, and secure.

This role will introduce you to the tax preparation business, where you will join our teams that are delivering on the many opportunities present to optimize and transform our services. You will partner with stakeholders across our business units to establish processes to ensure the effective management of data assets. Your passion for information management will lead you to identify opportunities for improvements, implement solutions that deliver positive change, and strengthen the organization’s data management maturity.

This position is based in Calgary and offers a hybrid work schedule, with 3 days per week in-office.

Main Responsibilities:
Develops and implements the data governance framework, including policies, standards, and procedures to ensure data integrity and security, ensuring alignment with our overall corporate data strategy.
Operates data governance processes around access standardization, data store inventory, data flows and mapping, data classification, data quality, and retention.
Establishes and maintains information governance documentation, including the data dictionary and data catalog.
Provides subject matter expertise on information governance principles, best practices, and regulatory requirements.
Develops and delivers training programs on information governance, data quality, and data management practices.
Works closely with information owners, stewards, and business units to ensure adherence to information governance policies and standards.
Collaborates with IT teams and the global Information Governance team to evaluate, select, and implement data management tools such as MDM, data quality, data catalog, and data lineage solutions.
Conducts data quality assessments and implements remediation measures to improve data accuracy, completeness, and consistency.
Collaborates with the Security team and Privacy Officer to ensure compliance with information security and privacy regulations.
Supports the development and execution of a plan to maximize self-service analytics capabilities including reporting (e.g., Power BI).
Stays informed about industry trends, emerging technologies, and regulatory changes related to information governance.
Contributes to the development and implementation of the enterprise data strategy.
Manages and reports on a centralized scorecard of all audits and active findings. This includes ongoing audits with upcoming compliance deadlines and past audits with recommended remediation activities.
Coordinates with other IT and business leads on activities to fulfill audit requirements and remediate deficiencies.
Tracks and reports on the cost of audit activities.
Provides operational and project support (planned and ad-hoc) to business partners.

Key Qualifications:
Bachelor's degree in Computer Science, Information Management, or a related field.
A minimum of 5 years of experience in information/data governance roles.
Strong knowledge of data governance principles, frameworks, and best practices.
Familiarity with Canadian and other relevant data privacy and security regulations (e.g., GDPR, CCPA) and their implications for information governance.
Experience with data management tools such as MDM, data quality, data catalog, and data lineage solutions.
Experience with Data Governance tools (e.g., Purview, Alation, etc.).
Fluency in both English and French is an advantage.
Excellent analytical and problem-solving skills, with the ability to identify information governance issues and propose effective solutions.
Certificate in data management or information/data governance is an advantage.
Strong communication and collaboration skills, with the ability to engage and influence stakeholders at all levels of the organization.
Skilled in process modeling and experience with data modelling, enterprise relationship diagrams and solution architectural diagrams.
Experience and knowledge of relational database structures and possess the ability to trace data flow.
Experience creating formal documentation and diagrams which capture current state and recommended future state of business processes and systems.
Self-motivated and proactive, with the ability to work independently and prioritize tasks effectively.
Authentic, curious, creative, and innovative.
Excited and motivated to help people, especially our clients and field associates.
Excellent interpersonal skills – able to build strong relationships with and seen as a trusted partner amongst business leaders.

Roll up your sleeves and get stuff done. No one can be counted on to execute faster or better than you.
Identify opportunities and make them happen.

Experience:

5 years of experience in a high growth environment in data and/or financial analytics.
Very strong attention to detail, experience developing processes to remove human error.
Proficient in SQL and quantitative analysis, you can deep dive into large amounts of data, draw meaningful insights, dissect business issues and draw actionable conclusions.
Outcome-driven approach to developing recommendations and demonstrated ability to develop a story and execution plan to support our goals and objectives.
Exceptional communication (listening, written, and oral) skills with the ability to present findings and recommendations targeted to the audience in question.

Sr. EDMS (Engineering Document Management System) Data Migration Analyst Overview / Responsibilities Sr. EDMS Data Migration Analyst will assist the EDMS team with migrating all revisions of documents, and associated metadata, from SPO, PIMS, and networks drives.

A Typical Day

Developing document/ data cleansing strategies, action plans, reconciliation plans and scripts, Determining document/ data migration requirements. 
Developing document/ data management plan, Good experience in writing SQL, Loader, SQL, PLSQL, Functional experience in EDMS systems including Smart Plant Foundation, and Omega PIMS. 
Determining the validity of the values of the data elements, Reviewing and validating data relationships between tags and documents. 
Coordinating with document/ data owners to validate cleansed document/ data (e.g., reconciling orphaned project documents against as-built documents to determine if these records need to be migrated)
Defining roles and responsibilities for the data migration activities, Reviewing and providing comments and suggestions on the data management plan, data migration plan, checklist, timeline, and conversion report delivered. 
Documenting migration activity timelines for mock conversions and production deployment, Developing a data migration checklist and sign-off process to ensure completion of planned activities, Mapping the data in the format provided in conversion templates. 
Assisting with determining data migration security controls, Developing unit and end-to-end integration migration test plans (including testing for data extraction, transformation, data loading, and data validation), Solid experience with data transformation and data load testing. 
Validating data of multiple mock conversions and the full migration coordinating with unit and end-to-end integration testing to ensure the flow of data from the source applications to the target applications is accurate, Documenting the end-to-end data migration test results and lessons learned report. 

Successful Candidates Will Have

Education - MA/MS/BA/BS degree and 10 years of experience in supporting large data migration/conversion for EDMS applications. 
Communication - Good communication skills both written and verbal. Willing and able to resolve team conflicts. 
Leadership skills - Able to provide direction and oversight of EDMS migration activities and deliverables. 
Project Planning - Must have the ability to translate contractual requirements into EDMS migration project execution plans. 
Project Execution - Demonstrates interest and understanding of overall project workflow, project execution plan, procedures, and project primary deliverables and activities. 
Systems and Tools knowledge- Must have hands-on knowledge of the EDMS systems (SmartPlant Foundation, and Omega PIMS) and tools used to support EDMS migrations (SQL * Loader, SQL, PLSQL). 
Problem Solving skills - Demonstrate the ability to identify, analyze and resolve documentation and data issues in accordance with sound Information Management principles.

Who We Are

Geotab ® is a global leader in IoT and connected transportation and certified “Great Place to Work ™ .” We are a company of diverse and talented individuals who work together to help businesses grow and succeed, and increase the safety and sustainability of our communities.

Geotab is advancing security, connecting commercial vehicles to the internet and providing web-based analytics to help customers better manage their fleets. Geotab’s open platform and Geotab Marketplace ® , offering hundreds of third-party solution options, allows both small and large businesses to automate operations by integrating vehicle data with their other data assets. Who You Are

We are always looking for amazing talent who can contribute to our growth and deliver results! Geotab is seeking a Senior Data Analyst, Sustainability who will perform data analytics in order to support Geotab’s thought leadership related to electric vehicles and fleet. If you love technology, and are keen to join an industry leader — we would love to hear from you!

What You'll Do

The Senior Data Analyst, Sustainability will use strong problem-solving skills with statistical analysis in order to conduct queries, track reporting metrics and analyze data to support Geotab’s sustainability marketing and thought leadership goals. This role will be key in uncovering data-backed insights and proof points for marketing campaigns that help educate internal and external stakeholders on the topic of sustainable fleet and electric vehicles. To be successful in this role you will be a self-starter and problem solver with strong written and verbal communication skills, and have the ability to quickly understand complex, technical concepts.

How You’ll Make An Impact

Examine large data sets to identify trends, develop charts, and create visual presentations to help businesses make more strategic decisions.
Apply statistical methods toward data validation of Geotab aggregate traffic-related data against third-party data sources
Utilize statistical tools to interpret data sets and prepare reports and technical papers that effectively communicate trends, patterns, and predictions based on relevant findings.
Write SQL queries to find answers to complex business questions.
Identify any data quality issues and partialities in data acquisition.
Coordinate with engineering teams to gather incremental new data.
Process, cleanse, and verify the integrity of data used for analysis.
Use data mining, model building, and other analytical techniques to develop customer segmentation.
Work with data scientists and leverage machine learning models that have been developed against Geotab’s big data environment.

What You’ll Bring To This Role

Post-secondary Degree/Diploma specialization in Computer Science, Software Engineering, Science, Mathematics, or a related field.
5-8 years experience as a Data Analyst or a similar role.
5-8 years experience with SQL.
5-8 years experience with data science tools (e.g. Python, Pandas, NumPy) as well as BI tools such as Superset/Redash/PowerBI or tableau.
Experience working with big data and an understanding of techniques used to extract value out of very large datasets.
Familiarity with machine learning concepts is an asset.
Strong analytical skills with the ability to problem solve well-judged decisions.
Strategic mindset, with a keen sense of priorities, along with an ability to pivot as the landscape changes.
Strong team-player with the ability to engage with all levels of the organization.
Technical competence using software programs, including but not limited to, Google Suite for business (Sheets, Docs, Slides).
Strong communications and creativity skills with the ability to link data insights to marketing initiatives and use data to tell a story.
Knowledge and experience with GHG emissions reporting, electric vehicle data and fuel efficiency practices are highly valued. 
Proven experience in data cleaning, with the ability to identify, analyze, and interpret inconsistencies or inaccuracies in data.
Strong critical thinking abilities, with experience leveraging data to make well-informed recommendations and decisions.

Our Values

At TD we're guided by our purpose is to enrich the lives of our customers, communities and colleagues, and share a set of values that shape our culture and guide our behavior. Making Your Well-being a Priority

A supportive culture that promotes colleague well-being is core to who we are. At TD, we focus on total well-being with extensive programs to help colleagues assess, manage, and improve their well-being across four core pillars — physical, financial, social and mental/emotional. In addition, we champion a safe and inclusive work environment so colleagues feel a sense of belonging and feel supported in their personal and professional growth. Through our focus on well-being, we know that we can help our colleagues thrive, contribute to our culture of care, and support better business outcomes, because when colleagues feel their best, they're more likely to do their best.

Our Total Rewards Package

Our Total Rewards package reflects the investment we make in our colleagues to help them, and their families achieve their well-being goals. Total Rewards at TD includes a base salary, variable compensation, and several other key plans such as health and well-being benefits including medical, dental, vision & mental health coverage, savings and retirement programs, paid time off, banking benefits and discounts, career development, and reward and recognition programs.

How We Work

At TD, we believe in-person connections fuel collaboration and collective creativity. Our workplace experience empowers colleagues to do great work side-by-side at TD locations, while offering flexibility to work remotely where it makes sense for the work and team. Our teams work in one of three workplace models: Hybrid, Onsite and Primarily Remote. Wherever our colleagues are working, they’ll always have access to the TD community and experience our culture of care.

Job Description

Reporting to the Manager, Forecasting/ Planning, the successful candidate will be responsible for ensuring operational KPI targets and efficiency goals are met by providing the business with complete end-to-end Workforce Management (WFM) support. This position is responsible for producing an 18-month rolling forecast of contact center demand, capacity, service outlooks and productivity. The successful candidate will create compelling performance impact analysis, budget plans, and risk mitigation tactics to help support our operational business leaders.

Primary Responsibilities

Support business decisions through the preparation of accurate KPI forecasts, with specific focus on improving customer experience and maximizing operational efficiencies 
Provide detailed analysis on current & future market environments to help facilitate high-impact decision making process
Aggregate forecast information into comprehensive, executive level presentation material
Present analysis in a clear, concise manner with specific recommendations on how to improve Service Level and efficiency
Leverage statistical methodologies (regression, correlation etc.) to assess the impact of new market data 
Track KPI performance (e.g., service level, call volume, AHT, shrinkage etc.) to highlight performance trends
Assess short, medium, and long-term impacts of hiring, queue consolidation, attrition, digital automation, off/nearshoring and contingent labor
Support the maintenance & development of workforce planning tools / processes
Communicate effectively with internal and external stakeholders in accordance with TD's policies, guidelines, and procedures

Key Relationships

Reports to Manager, Forecasting/ Planning
Finance, Talent Acquisition, Learning & Development, Product & Strategic Initiative partners
Distribution & Contact Centre leaders across different locations
Daily working relationships with all level of TDBG

Job Requirements

Exceptional analytical skills with high attention to detail
Proficient with MS Office Suite (Excel, PowerPoint, Word)
Strong organizational skills with a proven ability to multitask
Ability to articulate reasons for forecast variance and recommend changes to enhance forecast accuracy and effectiveness
Clear and thorough understanding of short, medium, and long-term forecasting practices
Ability to quickly learn new technology/software/systems
Superior verbal and written communication skills
Driven to continual improvement of processes and working environment
Enjoys working in an agile, fast pace and collaborative environment

Additional Information

EDUCATION & WORK EXPERIENCE:

A post-secondary degree in business, economics, computers, or other related fields of study
3-5 years of experience in workforce management, planning, and analytics
Experience with database management and/or visualization software such as Tableau, Power BI, SQL is an asset. Good to have PHP, Python, R etc. 
Experience with Genesys Decisions forecasting software is an asset

Job Description:

PURPOSE OF POSITION

Accountable for the design, development and maintenance of department information resource files and manuals, conducting research and coordinating the development and publication of department information bulletins, newsletters and Website content for employees and internal stakeholders on licensing and registration legislation, policies, procedures, and processes of FSRA.

Note : This is a 12 Month Contract Position.

Key Responsibilities

Develops and maintains department resource information files, manuals and data base systems. Consults with department management and staff to identify resource needs for staff and clients, and researches, develops and implements resource information systems and processes.
Maintains computerized data bases of information about registrant companies/institutions.
Provides analytical support to management and staff by extracting, analyzing and preparing reports in response to internal information requests.
Provides input to the preparation of the annual report by extracting reporting data from data bases, checking for accuracy, and submitting to the staff member coordinating publication of the annual report.
Provides information research and analysis support to the manager and assists in the preparation of section reports and briefings. Undertakes special projects as assigned.
 Monitors and analyzes data for the life licence qualifications program. Logs problems and necessary data system amendments and works with other areas of FSRA or approved data system projects as department liaison.
Coordinates assembly and preparation of information from department staff, and designs/develops newsletters and information bulletins for department stakeholder sectors on legislation and policies, and licensing/registration requirements, procedures, and processes. Coordinates the preparation of mass mailings.
Develops web content related to department services/processes and monitors the site to ensure integrity and accuracy of information.
Conducts research of information and preparation of responses related to requests under legislation governing freedom of information.

Qualifications

Education and Experience 

Diploma/degree in Records Management, Information Management or a related field.
3 – 4 years of experience developing and maintaining electronic filing systems.

Knowledge And Skills

Knowledge of information management systems, procedures, practices, and processes to establish and maintain electronic filing systems.
General understanding of the legislation governing FSRA’s policies and licensing/registration processes and systems to prepare information bulletins and newsletters for use by internal/external clients, and to update website information.
Knowledge of the Freedom of Information and Protection of Privacy Act (FIPPA) to research and prepare responses for information inquiries.
Knowledge of business operations of client registrant companies to ensure that published information meets the business needs of stakeholder clients.
Research skills to conduct research assignments and projects.
Strong analytical skills with the ability to collect, organize, analyze, and disseminate significant amounts of information with attention to detail and accuracy.
Ability to prioritize and handle multiple tasks in a fast-paced environment with attention to detail and accuracy.
Interpersonal skills and the ability to tactfully communicate with various levels, internally and externally, to request or provide information.
Ability to develop and maintain collaborative working relationships, while demonstrating a high level of cooperation and mutual respect.
Written and verbal communication to gather information from staff for the preparation of newsletters and information bulletins, and to prepare information bulletins, newsletters, and research summaries/reports.
Proficient with Microsoft Office (Word, Excel, PowerPoint, SharePoint, Teams) and other internal applications, as required.

What You'll Do

Supervise and mentor a team of data analysts, providing guidance on best practices, methodologies, and professional development.

Implement and maintain data governance practices to ensure compliance with industry standards and regulations.

Oversee the design and delivery of reports and insights, analyzing business functions, key operations, and performance metrics.
Manage the design, development, and maintenance of ongoing metrics, reports, analyses, and dashboards to steer key business decisions.
Facilitate the organization's transition from prescriptive to predictive analytics by developing relevant processes and products.
Serve as a Subject Matter Expert (SME), extending guidance to team members and participating in departmental and cross-departmental projects while showcasing expert project leadership.
Collaborate with cross-functional teams including product managers, data engineers, data analysts, data scientists, and developers,to gather requirements and build data products.
Promote knowledge sharing within the team, avoiding potential single points of failure, and utilizing influence without authority to tackle technical impediments

What You’ll Bring To This Role

Masters or equivalent degree in Computer Science, Computer Engineering, Electrical Engineering, Data Science or a related field.
8-10 years experience as a Data Analyst, Data Scientist, or a similar role.
8-10 years experience in programming in Python.
Experience in working with large amounts of data in SQL.
Experience with designing and implementing monitoring and alert systems.
Proven experience in machine learning model development for anomaly detection.
Solid understanding of statistical analysis, quantitative analytics, forecasting/predictive analytics, and multivariate testing.
Experience with model deployment in large-scale production systems.
Proficient in building models using TensorFlow, Keras, PyTorch, scikit-learn. 
Experience with AirFlow, BigQuery, docker, kubernetes and other cloud based technologies to scale machine learning models.

Ce poste exige une personne qui peut travailler de manière autonome, mais également au sein d'une équipe, qui est motivée, qui a d'excellentes aptitudes à la communication et qui a une grande expérience en analyse de données.

What your day will look like:
Design and develop enterprise and departmental business intelligence and reporting solutions
Collect business requirements from stakeholders
Develop and implement ETL processes and queries in support of business analytics
Design reports and dashboards in Power BI containing metrics that clearly communicate business performance and effectively communicate trends, patterns, and predictions using relevant data and suggest data-driven interventions

Design and carry-out experiments to test analyses based on business assumptions or assess the impact of interventions

About the job
Flipp is a pre-IPO company on a mission to help shoppers provide for their families by making life more affordable by leveraging technology. We work with the largest retailers and manufacturers in the world to help them transform their businesses and connect them with millions of shoppers through our next-generation digital shopping marketplace. Our award-winning Flipp app is used by millions of shoppers every week to make better purchase decisions and to save 20-40% off their bills.

With the recent increase in costs of living, Flipp’s mission has never been more relevant. Flipp’s Shopper Consideration Platform allows retailers and manufacturers to create digital experiences from their savings & deals content. These experiences help Shoppers decide what to buy and where to buy it. Flipp then connects those retailer and manufacturer experiences to millions of shoppers through Flipp’s owned and operated channels.

As a Partner Insights Analyst, you'll get the opportunity to act as a trusted advisor for our internal sales & product team members in support of our retail partners. You'll leverage data & insights to drive strategy, formulate business actions and maximize demonstrated business results. You'll also communicate and coordinate plans with our internal sales and product teams to drive our business forward.

Experience with data visualization and reporting (eg. Thoughtspot, Tableau, Periscope, Domo, Amplitude, etc.)

A passion for constant improvement; always looking to do things better (both personally, as part of a team and for the company)
A quick learner, with an open-minded perspective to understand Flipp’s disciplined approach

Understanding of the retail, CPG, loyalty, consumer analysis, and digital media domain is preferred

About The Role

CrowdStrike Intelligence, a core component of CrowdStrike Counter Adversary Operations, is seeking to hire a Senior Intelligence Analyst for its Intelligence Analysis Cell (IAC) to focus on eCrime. This position will primarily conduct analysis on established and emerging actors in the eCrime ecosystem, criminal operating models, monetization techniques, and the geographic diversity of eCrime. This position is instrumental in providing unique insight into the strategic context and operating environment of adversaries through finished intelligence products used by CrowdStrike customers and stakeholders.

What You'll Do

Analyze financially-motivated cyber actors and compose long- and short-form finished intelligence reports related to actor tracking, monetization methods, commodity and closed malware groups, and fraud techniques
Research, assess, and report on specific cyber threat actor and adversary capabilities, motivations, and Tactics, Techniques, and Procedures (TTPs)
Provide clear and concise written responses to customer requests for information (RFIs) and contribute to briefings where necessary
Work in a collaborative environment with other analysts, technical experts, and customer-facing personnel
Assist in research prioritization efforts and intelligence gap identification

What You'll Need

5+ years’ experience conducting research in the field of eCrime to include producing intelligence assessments and handling ad-hoc requests for information (RFIs)
A strong understanding of current and emerging threats related to financially-motivated computer intrusions, scams, and fraud techniques
In-depth knowledge of current underground criminal forums and marketplaces, digital currency use in criminal activity, enabling infrastructures, monetization methods, money laundering, and access brokers
A general understanding of commonly used criminal malware, botnets, and access brokers
An ability to express complex technical and non-technical concepts verbally, graphically, and in writing
Excellent English writing and open-source research skills
Comprehensive practical knowledge of intelligence analysis and collection skills
An analytic mindset capable of applying best practices such as structured analysis, awareness of biases and other pitfalls, and critical thinking in source evaluation
Undergraduate degree in cybersecurity, general intelligence studies, security studies, criminal justice, political science, international relations; or equivalent military training and experience in a cyber intelligence/security MOS
Technical and non-technical security certifications pertaining to financial crimes analysis, anti-money laundering (AML), or cyber threat intelligence

Preferred

Graduate or professional degrees in any of the aforementioned fields
Ability to utilize graph analysis tools (e.g., i2 Analyst Notebook, Maltego) to create both working-level and presentation-grade visualization charts
Experience contributing to Computer Network Operations (CNO) campaign tracking, including working with technical indicators pertaining to malware and network infrastructure
Formal foreign language training or competency, especially in Russian, Farsi, Chinese, Spanish, or Portuguese

 Analyste des données 

 Direction générale : Direction générale des ressources informationnelles et de la transformation numérique (DGRITN)

 Les défis que nous vous proposons 

La DGDIA est une toute nouvelle direction qui a la responsabilité de coordonner la gouvernance et la valorisation des données pour le Ministère et d’assurer le développement de l’automatisation et de l’intelligence artificielle aux différents secteurs d’affaires. Chez nous, vous trouverez un environnement de travail stimulant, des possibilités d’apprentissage en continu, une culture organisationnelle axée sur l’excellence et un climat de travail des plus agréables. Votre prochaine grande aventure professionnelle commence ici! En tant qu’analyste des données, vous serez responsable de la collecte, de l’analyse et de l’interprétation des données dans le contexte de projets d’intelligence artificielle. Dans votre rôle, vous aurez à :

 Analyser les besoins, les préoccupations, les enjeux et les problématiques de la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Définir, concevoir et mettre en place des mesures et des indicateurs liés à la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Tenir des registres précis des activités liées aux données, des méthodes utilisées et des résultats obtenus afin de garantir la reproductibilité et la transparence des travaux ; 
 Participer au choix des caractéristiques et variables les plus pertinentes à inclure dans les modèles afin d’améliorer les performances de l’intelligence artificielle ; 
 Promouvoir les bonnes pratiques, les normes et les standards au sein des solutions d’intelligence artificielle pour répondre au besoin de visualisation et de présentation de l’information ; 
 Garantir la qualité des résultats obtenus et contribuer à la certification des produits informationnels en soutenant la standardisation des méthodes d’exploitation des données ; 
 Assurer le lien de la gestion des données entre les secteurs d’affaires et les RI ; 
 Participer, en collaboration avec les ressources informationnelles, à la création des produits informationnels afin de permettre une utilisation conviviale et documenter les portées de ceux-ci.

 Apprends-en davantage sur nous : 

 FAIRE CARRIÈRE AU MINISTÈRE DES TRANSPORTS ET DE LA MOBILITÉ DURABLE 

Les défis à relever sont nombreux et stimulants. Intervenant de premier plan dans l’économie du Québec, le Ministère a pour mission et mandat d’assurer, sur l’ensemble de son territoire, la mobilité durable des personnes et des marchandises par des systèmes de transport efficaces et sécuritaires. Vaste organisation, le Ministère emploie plus de 8 500 personnes et gère 31 000 kilomètres de routes et 11 000 structures. Concrètement, le Ministère entretient, rend sécuritaires, conçoit et bâtit les vastes réseaux de transport maritime, ferroviaire, aérien et routier du Québec tout en innovant et en respectant l’environnement.

 LA DIRECTION DE LA GOUVERNANCE DES DONNÉES ET DE L’INTELLIGENCE ARTIFICIELLE (DVGDIA) 

La DGDIA conseille la haute direction et les utilisateurs sur l’utilisation optimale des données et des technologies d’IA. Son mandat est de développer, améliorer, entretenir et exploiter les technologies de l’information liées aux données et à l’IA pour soutenir la mission du Ministère et répondre à ses besoins. La direction élabore et promeut des normes, politiques et directives pour l’automatisation et l’utilisation responsable de l’IA, veillant à l’intégrité et à la sécurité des données. Elle encourage l’innovation en promouvant l’adoption de nouvelles technologies et en favorisant l’échange d’idées. Elle assure un rôle de surveillance pour s’assurer que l’utilisation des données et de l’IA respecte les lois et politiques en vigueur, établissant des mécanismes de contrôle et de vérification.

Role Summary

As a Data Analyst for Payroll Implementation, your primary responsibility will be to analyze and interpret data related to the implementation of a new payroll system. You will work closely with the project team to gather and validate data, perform data cleansing and transformation, and provide insights and recommendations based on your analysis.

Key Responsibilities

 Collaborate with the project team to understand data requirements for the payroll system implementation.
 Gather, validate, and analyze data from various sources, ensuring data accuracy and completeness.
 Perform data cleansing and transformation to ensure data consistency and integrity.
 Develop and maintain data models, reports, and dashboards to visualize and present data analysis findings.
 Identify trends, patterns, and anomalies in data, and provide insights and recommendations to optimize payroll processes.
 Work closely with stakeholders to understand their data analysis needs and provide customized reports and analysis.
 Collaborate with IT teams to ensure data integration and migration from legacy systems to the new payroll system.
 Perform data validation and reconciliation to ensure data accuracy and consistency between different systems.
 Assist in the development and implementation of data quality control measures to ensure data integrity.
 Stay updated with industry best practices and trends in data analysis and implement them in the payroll implementation process.



Key Qualifications/Requirements

 Bachelor's degree in Data Science, Statistics, Computer Science, or a related field.
 Proven experience as a data analyst or similar role, preferably in the payroll domain.
 Strong proficiency in data analysis and visualization tools such as SQL, Excel, Power BI, or Tableau.
 Excellent data manipulation and data cleansing skills.
 Knowledge of database management systems, data warehousing, and data integration concepts.
 Strong analytical and problem-solving skills.
 Ability to interpret complex data and present insights in a clear and concise manner.
 Strong attention to detail and accuracy in data analysis.
 Ability to work effectively in a team and collaborate with cross-functional stakeholders.
 Knowledge of payroll processes, systems, and compliance requirements is an asset.

Description

Position Summary

The Data Analysis Supervisor oversees a regional data analysis staff ensuring on time delivery and highly accurate reports are issued that consistently exceed customer expectations. Demonstrated ability to lead a mid-sized to large team, aligning processes, workflows, deliverables, timeliness, HSE and Quality with internal and customer needs. Performs administrative tasks, such as approving timesheets for assigned group and maintaining vacation records for personnel. Long term focus on scalability and sustainability, in accordance with Entegra’s vision for global growth.

Primary Responsibilities

Safety shall always be the top priority.
Work in a team environment collaborating and sharing knowledge and experience.
Supervise day to day activity of regional Data Analysis personnel.
Prioritize workload and resources ensuring on time delivery of all reports.
Ensure efficient and effective workflow creating scalable systems.
Ensure capacity to meet Strategic Growth needs and commitment to Customers.
Drive the highest quality reports by ensuring quality checks are in place and personnel are diligently focused on exceeding customer expectations.
Lead continuous improvement in identification, location, recognition, classification, sizing, accuracy, and visualization of integrity threats based on field correlation.
Attends client performance meetings, seek client feedback on team performance, implement improvements to ensure client requirements and expectations are being met.
Understand and drive compliance with API 1163, ASNT ILI-PQ, and POF. 
Occasionally perform Data Quality Assessments (DQA) and provide reports to clients meeting their required timelines.
Performs QA/QC checks when requested to do so for DQAs, Preliminary Final Reports and any other client-based reports that require verification.
Aid Sales, Engineering, Project Management and Operations with risk assessments of future ILI surveys regarding the feasibility of Entegra tools to successfully navigate and collect data from a Data Analyst point of view.
Assist Operations and Engineering the collection of tool data results for RCA documentation.
Assist in standardizing processes and procedures.

About The Role

We are seeking a passionate competitive intelligence/field professional to support our product and sales teams. This role will function as the competitive product leader within CrowdStrike for Falcon for IT.

In this role you will be directly working with our product teams to guide roadmap decisions by developing a deep, nuanced understanding of the competition’s technical capabilities, primary GTM strategy/tactics, as well as why CrowdStrike wins or loses vs. the competition in visibility and automation in IT and security workflows. You will partner with senior leaders across Product Groups, Sales, Enablement, and Marketing to achieve these objectives and scale to a global level.

This role requires deep technical knowledge in IT cyber security, and a functional understanding of actual real-world deployments, extended use-cases, and customer motivations. Make recommendations on sales tactics and product strategy to enable CrowdStrike to win in the market.

This is an individual contributor, remote work position.

What You’ll Do

You will be required to synthesize and formulate guidance from a variety of information levels and sources (technical, business, field, external) and regularly present key takeaways to the field and to senior leadership

Provide tailored deal support (competitive surgeries & guidance), and develop a deep rapport with the field
You will work closely with the rest of the Competitive Intelligence team at CrowdStrike, as well as other key stakeholders (including the office of the CTO, field leadership, sales ops, product, and marketing teams), functioning as a primary liaison for IT Ops competition which includes development of competitive support material and competitive readiness plans
Make recommendations on sales tactics and product strategy to enable CrowdStrike to win in the market
Will be expected to be a self-starter with an ownership mentality. You will work autonomously in the development of project plans, requirements, timelines, content, and ongoing tracking/updates of the IT competitive landscape.

About The Role

CrowdStrike Intelligence, a core component of CrowdStrike Counter Adversary Operations, is seeking to hire a Senior Intelligence Analyst for its Intelligence Analysis Cell (IAC) to focus on eCrime. This position will primarily conduct analysis on established and emerging actors in the eCrime ecosystem, criminal operating models, monetization techniques, and the geographic diversity of eCrime. This position is instrumental in providing unique insight into the strategic context and operating environment of adversaries through finished intelligence products used by CrowdStrike customers and stakeholders.

What You'll Do

Analyze financially-motivated cyber actors and compose long- and short-form finished intelligence reports related to actor tracking, monetization methods, commodity and closed malware groups, and fraud techniques
Research, assess, and report on specific cyber threat actor and adversary capabilities, motivations, and Tactics, Techniques, and Procedures (TTPs)
Provide clear and concise written responses to customer requests for information (RFIs) and contribute to briefings where necessary
Work in a collaborative environment with other analysts, technical experts, and customer-facing personnel
Assist in research prioritization efforts and intelligence gap identification

What You'll Need

5+ years’ experience conducting research in the field of eCrime to include producing intelligence assessments and handling ad-hoc requests for information (RFIs)
A strong understanding of current and emerging threats related to financially-motivated computer intrusions, scams, and fraud techniques
In-depth knowledge of current underground criminal forums and marketplaces, digital currency use in criminal activity, enabling infrastructures, monetization methods, money laundering, and access brokers
A general understanding of commonly used criminal malware, botnets, and access brokers
An ability to express complex technical and non-technical concepts verbally, graphically, and in writing
Excellent English writing and open-source research skills
Comprehensive practical knowledge of intelligence analysis and collection skills
An analytic mindset capable of applying best practices such as structured analysis, awareness of biases and other pitfalls, and critical thinking in source evaluation
Undergraduate degree in cybersecurity, general intelligence studies, security studies, criminal justice, political science, international relations; or equivalent military training and experience in a cyber intelligence/security MOS
Technical and non-technical security certifications pertaining to financial crimes analysis, anti-money laundering (AML), or cyber threat intelligence

Preferred

Graduate or professional degrees in any of the aforementioned fields
Ability to utilize graph analysis tools (e.g., i2 Analyst Notebook, Maltego) to create both working-level and presentation-grade visualization charts
Experience contributing to Computer Network Operations (CNO) campaign tracking, including working with technical indicators pertaining to malware and network infrastructure
Formal foreign language training or competency, especially in Russian, Farsi, Chinese, Spanish, or Portuguese

Exercise good judgment to promptly resolve and/or escalate problems/discrepancies within established timelines and document clearly all occurrences and exceptions for future reference.

Job Description

Reporting to the Manager of Operations Finance, the Data Analyst II is responsible for transforming raw data into actionable insights that contribute to strategic decision-making. This role works closely with cross-functional teams to analyze large datasets, identify trends, and communicate findings to stakeholders.

Note: This position qualifies for an optional hybrid work schedule after 90 days of onsite work and onboarding. Employee will be subject to the terms of the Flexible Work Policy Agreement.

What You’ll Do

Power BI Development:

Designs, develops, and maintains interactive and visually compelling Power BI dashboards and reports tailored to the unique requirements of the shipbuilding industry.
Creates data models and data structures within Power BI to ensure efficient data organization and retrieval. Implement data transformations, calculations, and aggregations to support analysis and reporting needs.
Integrates data from different sources into Power BI, ensuring data accuracy and consistency. 
Generates regular reports and ad-hoc analyses using Power BI. Customize reports based on stakeholder requirements and provide insights to support decision-making processes.


Data Analysis And Interpretation

Analyzes complex data sets related to shipbuilding projects, design and production processes, and performance metrics to identify trends, patterns, and areas for improvement.
Provides insights and recommendations to enhance operational efficiency, cost-effectiveness, and overall project success.


Collaboration

Collaborates with cross-functional teams, including engineering, project management, and finance, to understand data requirements and deliver solutions that meet business needs.
Communicates findings and insights in a clear and understandable manner to both technical and non-technical stakeholders.
Proactively identifies opportunities for process improvement and automation.


Data Governance

Ensures the integrity, security, and quality of data through effective data governance practices.
Establishes and enforce data standards and best practices within the shipbuilding data environment.


What You’ll Bring

Bachelor’s degree in a quantitative field such as Statistics, Mathematics, Computer Science, Economics, or a related discipline. 
Minimum of 3 years of experience as a data analyst.
Proven experience as a Data Analyst or in a similar role.
Proficiency in DAX (Data Analysis Expressions) is a valuable skill for a Data Analyst, as it enables efficient manipulation and analysis of data within Microsoft Power BI and Excel.
Proficient in data analysis tools and languages (e.g., SQL, Python, R) is a plus.
Strong analytical and problem-solving skills with a keen attention to detail.
Experience with data visualization tools such as Power BI.
Excellent communication skills with the ability to convey complex findings to non-technical stakeholders.
Familiarity with database management concepts.
Ability to work independently and collaboratively in a fast-paced environment.
Familiarity with Finance Environment is a plus.

About the job
Position Job Title: Junior Data Analyst
Location: Vancouver, BC (Hybrid)
Reports To: Business Intelligence Analyst
Application Requirement: Cover Letter

Primary Purpose
Under the guidance of the Business Intelligence Analyst, the Junior Data Analyst ensures the integrity of the university’s enrolment management data through monitoring accuracy and participating in initiatives aimed at both streamlining data entry processes and improving overall efficacy as well as providing resources and support as required for data-entry staff to perform their jobs effectively. Additionally, they support the preparation of reports, presentations, and other documents that communicate data findings to various stakeholders.

Specific Responsibilities
Ensure the accuracy of data in the student management system by conducting regular audits to clean data, fill gaps, and reduce data disparity.
Identify issues in data entry processes that lead to errors, collaborating with appropriate staff and/or supervisors to address resolutions in a timely manner.
Support data entry staff and/or supervisors with queries regarding system issues, reporting needs, and/or questions.
Support the development and revision of reporting processes for increased automation and efficacy.
Facilitate the preparation of data-driven reports from multiple systems, summarizing and preparing the visualization of data.

*This job description outlines the key responsibilities for the role and is not meant to be exhaustive. Other responsibilities and tasks may be assigned or may naturally become a part of this role over time.

Position Requirements
To be successful in the Junior Data Analyst position, the individual must be committed to developing, maintaining, and demonstrating the following:

Competencies:
Strong attention to detail, ensuring accuracy with decision-making and data records.
Efficient, effective, and dependable time management skills in order to multitask, with flexibility to handle changing priorities.
Demonstrated skills in cross-cultural communications and to relate both constructively and professionally with students, faculty, staff and external partners.
A high level of ethics, discretion, and tact.
An ability to work independently with minimal supervision.
Knowledge of concepts and processes related to higher education institutions.
Strong computer literacy, including full competency in Microsoft Office programs.

Education and experience:
Bachelor’s degree (preferably in a quantitative field such as Statistics, Mathematics, Computer Science, etc.) from a recognized post-secondary institution.
Experience in using MS Power BI (and/or other data analytical software) is preferable.
Or a combination of education and experience directly related and/or supportive to the duties and responsibilities.

To apply, please attach your cover letter and resume in a single PDF document to indicate how you are meeting the Education and Experience requirements.

 Analyste des données 

 Direction générale : Direction générale des ressources informationnelles et de la transformation numérique (DGRITN) 
 Direction générale adjointe : Direction générale adjointe de la gouvernance, de la sécurité informationnelle et de l’intelligence artificielle 
 Direction : Direction de la gouvernance des données et de l’intelligence artificielle (DGDIA) 
 Nombre d’emplois à pourvoir : 1 
 Statut de l’emploi : Régulier 
 Lieu de travail : 900 boulevard René-Lévesque Est, Québec* 
 Télétravail : en mode hybride 
 Horaire de travail : 35 heures par semaine 
 Date prévue d’entrée en fonction : Février 2024 
Étant un ministère qui œuvre partout sur le territoire et considérant la situation actuelle, nous avons l’opportunité de pourvoir cet emploi dans n’importe quelle région où il se trouve un bureau du ministère des Transports et la Mobilité durable

 Les défis que nous vous proposons 

La DGDIA est une toute nouvelle direction qui a la responsabilité de coordonner la gouvernance et la valorisation des données pour le Ministère et d’assurer le développement de l’automatisation et de l’intelligence artificielle aux différents secteurs d’affaires. Chez nous, vous trouverez un environnement de travail stimulant, des possibilités d’apprentissage en continu, une culture organisationnelle axée sur l’excellence et un climat de travail des plus agréables. Votre prochaine grande aventure professionnelle commence ici! En tant qu’analyste des données, vous serez responsable de la collecte, de l’analyse et de l’interprétation des données dans le contexte de projets d’intelligence artificielle. Dans votre rôle, vous aurez à :

 Analyser les besoins, les préoccupations, les enjeux et les problématiques de la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Définir, concevoir et mettre en place des mesures et des indicateurs liés à la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Tenir des registres précis des activités liées aux données, des méthodes utilisées et des résultats obtenus afin de garantir la reproductibilité et la transparence des travaux ; 
 Participer au choix des caractéristiques et variables les plus pertinentes à inclure dans les modèles afin d’améliorer les performances de l’intelligence artificielle ; 
 Promouvoir les bonnes pratiques, les normes et les standards au sein des solutions d’intelligence artificielle pour répondre au besoin de visualisation et de présentation de l’information ; 
 Garantir la qualité des résultats obtenus et contribuer à la certification des produits informationnels en soutenant la standardisation des méthodes d’exploitation des données ; 
 Assurer le lien de la gestion des données entre les secteurs d’affaires et les RI ; 
 Participer, en collaboration avec les ressources informationnelles, à la création des produits informationnels afin de permettre une utilisation conviviale et documenter les portées de ceux-ci.

 Apprends-en davantage sur nous : 

 FAIRE CARRIÈRE AU MINISTÈRE DES TRANSPORTS ET DE LA MOBILITÉ DURABLE 

Les défis à relever sont nombreux et stimulants. Intervenant de premier plan dans l’économie du Québec, le Ministère a pour mission et mandat d’assurer, sur l’ensemble de son territoire, la mobilité durable des personnes et des marchandises par des systèmes de transport efficaces et sécuritaires. Vaste organisation, le Ministère emploie plus de 8 500 personnes et gère 31 000 kilomètres de routes et 11 000 structures. Concrètement, le Ministère entretient, rend sécuritaires, conçoit et bâtit les vastes réseaux de transport maritime, ferroviaire, aérien et routier du Québec tout en innovant et en respectant l’environnement.

 LA DIRECTION DE LA GOUVERNANCE DES DONNÉES ET DE L’INTELLIGENCE ARTIFICIELLE (DVGDIA) 

La DGDIA conseille la haute direction et les utilisateurs sur l’utilisation optimale des données et des technologies d’IA. Son mandat est de développer, améliorer, entretenir et exploiter les technologies de l’information liées aux données et à l’IA pour soutenir la mission du Ministère et répondre à ses besoins. La direction élabore et promeut des normes, politiques et directives pour l’automatisation et l’utilisation responsable de l’IA, veillant à l’intégrité et à la sécurité des données. Elle encourage l’innovation en promouvant l’adoption de nouvelles technologies et en favorisant l’échange d’idées. Elle assure un rôle de surveillance pour s’assurer que l’utilisation des données et de l’IA respecte les lois et politiques en vigueur, établissant des mécanismes de contrôle et de vérification.

Job Summary

The focus of the role is to lead the development, aggregation, and documentation of business logic and calculation methodologies for sustainability data across the organization. This individual will sit within the Sustainability Program Office (SPO) and will work cross-functionally to develop internal requirements for the sustainability data lake, create data models for managing the corporate GHG inventory, and partner with the product team to define the logic for allocation of environmental data flows (carbon, water, etc) to customers. Candidates will be familiar with agile & sprint project management, ELT (extract, transform, load) pipelines, working in structured and non-structured data bases, as well as have experience with Power BI & Tableau.

Responsibilities

Responsible for developing & documenting business logic and calculation methodologies for sustainability and environmental data 
Cross-functionally collaborate with the product development team to create an organization-wide data lake for sustainability and environmental data 
Own prioritization and pipelines for data configuration & modeling 
Define and document requirements for environmental sustainability dashboard creation 
Drive customer support sustainability data issues to resolution 
Support the creation of feature validation test cases for sustainability products 
Partner with customer-facing teams, the SPO, Business Development, and Marketing to translate future customer sustainability data requirements into product features 
Expectation to grow into an expert on data center, real estate and technology-related sustainability topics including deep expertise in technical sustainability concepts relevant to Equinix’s industry 

Qualifications

1+ years of experience in sustainability 
3+ years of experience in data science, analytics, or product 
2+ years of experience with Power BI & Tableau preferred but not required 
Bachelor’s degree or equivalent in environmental science, statistics, mathematics, accounting, data science, or relevant STEM discipline required 
Master’s or MBA preferred but not required 
Familiar with ETL (extract, transform, load) pipelines and working with both structured and non-structured datasets 
Strong attention to detail and the ability to translate complex sustainability topics to a broad range of audiences 
Working knowledge of sustainability programs specific to energy, environment and emissions (e.g. CDP, GRI, The Greenhouse Gas Protocol, Science-based Targets Initiative, etc.) 
Demonstrated ability to manage multiple work streams with competing and sometimes urgent deadlines and experience influencing upwards to keep programs and projects moving 
Communicate clearly and effectively: verbally, in writing and through presentations; successfully interfacing with internal and external constituents
