Role Summary

Reporting to the Director, Data & Analytics (Insurance Solutions), the Business Intelligence Specialist will join a team of data scientists, data engineers, and analysts responsible for delivering data and analytical tools to support Sun Life’s individual insurance business in Canada.

The successful candidate will have a front row seat in shaping Sun Life Canada’s business intelligence capabilities, leading various analytics initiatives, and delivering innovative solutions to colleagues across product management, insurance distribution, actuarial, and innovation.

Insurance Solutions is one of the largest business units within Sun Life Canada, accounting for approximately 15% of worldwide earnings. We manufacture and distribute leading-edge life and health insurance products to over two million individual customers.

This is a one year contract role that offers partial benefits and vacation.

What will you do?

Design and Visualization

Design and facilitate workshops to understand user needs, set business requirements, and test BI dashboard designs with users
Translate user needs into compelling BI dashboard designs utilizing best practices in infographic design and aligned with Sun Life design language
Illustrate alternative concepts by mocking up sketches or wireframes with consistent and professional layout and visual; rapidly iterate and develop final versions

Data, Technology, and Tools

Develop metrics and KPIs to measure the performance of analytical and data products in the overall portfolio.
Responsible for improving the quality and management of data assets across distribution, finance, actuarial, product domains
Partner with different partners in the team, business, and IT to evolve data foundation and technology stack for Insurance Solutions
Assist in the migration of all of BI and Insights data foundation to the Enterprise Data Lake

Project and Relationship Management

Build and maintain strong working relationships with the Distribution, Pricing, Operations and IT partners to ensure delivery of initiatives within the area.
Design and deliver end-user training and training materials; provide technical support as necessary
Perform voice of the customer (VOC) feedback analysis to gain insights, take actions and improve.

What will you need to succeed?

4+ years of experience in data analytics with a focus on business intelligence
3+ years of experience and strong understanding of best practices in data visualization and dashboard design
4+ years of experience in Data Visualization tools, atleast 2 years working with Tableau
2+ years of experience with data querying languages (SQL)and techniques, analysis tools, data sources and structures
Excellent verbal and written communication, interpersonal and teamwork skills
Experience in insurance and financial service industry is an asset, but not required
Knowledge in one or more programming languages (Python/R)
Education background in math/UI design/statistics/financial engineering/data analytics

What is in it for you?

Competitive salary influenced by market range data
A friendly, collaborative and inclusive culture
Being part of our Analytics community, where we share best practices and broaden skill-sets

About the job
Trace la courbe de ta carrière dans l'équipe Innovation

Nous offrons un accompagnement technologique et des services techniques aux entreprises québécoises qui leur permettent d’innover et d’augmenter leur productivité de façon intelligente et durable. De plus, nos conseillers industriels accompagnent les entreprises dans l’identification et la priorisation de leurs besoins technologiques, les mettent en relation avec des ressources internes et externes et assurent le suivi des projets auprès des clients.

Le rôle: 

L’analyste en informations normatives et de marché est spécialisé dans le domaine des exigences normatives et de marchés pour les produits manufacturiers. Le titulaire doit, entre autres, accompagner les entreprises manufacturières qui souhaitent entreprendre un projet qui nécessite de connaître les exigences normatives des marchés d’exportations envisagés.

Les principales responsabilités: 

Analyser les besoins d’accompagnement des entreprises manufacturières en regard des aspects normatifs et de marchés d’un projet d’exportation et établir une proposition d’accompagnement;
Étudier les caractéristiques techniques des produits manufacturiers visés par un projet d’exportation;
Collecter, analyser et synthétiser des données normatives et de marchés afin de produire une information à valeur ajoutée en regard de chaque produit manufacturier étudié;
Répondre aux demandes d’informations techniques des entreprises en les orientant vers des normes, lois et règlements touchant leurs produits manufacturiers, tant pour le Canada que pour d’autres pays;
Produire des rapports, des bulletins, des conclusions et/ou des réponses, les livrer et en assurer la présentation et le suivi auprès des entreprises;
Effectuer la gestion de projets d’accompagnement;
Réaliser des présentations/conférences/formations en lien avec les aspects normatifs de l’exportation et/ou l’acceptation de produits;
Maintenir à jour ses connaissances au niveau des normes, lois et règlements touchant les secteurs manufacturiers canadiens et étrangers;
Entretenir et développer des relations d’affaires avec les organismes normatifs, les laboratoires canadiens et étrangers et des intervenants/experts dans les différents marchés d’exportation;
Accomplir, au besoin, toute autre tâche nécessaire au bon fonctionnement de l’organisation. 

Les qualifications requises:

Baccalauréat en génie mécanique ou dans une discipline connexe

Avoir des connaissances et de l’expertise reliées à l’analyse de quantité importante de documents;

Field Competitive Intelligence Analyst, Americas (Remote CT/MT) 

About The Role

As a Field Competitive Intelligence Analyst, you will support the CrowdStrike Sales and Executive Teams. You will work and support the CTO Labs and Field CTO Teams team at CrowdStrike. The Field CI team’s mission is to identify & deliver key competitive differentiators to support the international growth of customers, new markets, and TAM. This includes driving strategy through cross functional collaboration across the company including Product, Sales, Marketing, and more.

As the Field CI Analyst, you will be responsible for creating and communicating the company’s competitive differentiation strategy on a regional basis and working closely with the company’s product CTO’s, Product Managers and Field functions on a regular basis. You will also work closely with other groups within CrowdStrike, which includes: marketing, value management, legal and corporate affairs teams.

This role reports to the Manager, Competitive Intelligence Strategy. With your extensive cybersecurity background and your ability to think and operate at a strategic level, you will drive CrowdStrike’s technical vision and strategy and support on strategic engagements across the CrowdStrike organization.

What You'll Do

Support current customers and new customers by sharing CrowdStrike’s key competitive value differentiators, supporting the positioning of CrowdStrike as the leading thought leader for Cybersecurity with customers, partners, and analysts.
Driving and communicating CrowdStrike’s technology strategy to customers and partners as well as industry events.
Maintaining an in-depth knowledge of the cyber security industry, the competitive landscape and related industry developments to ensure we continue to be thought leaders who innovate ahead of the market.
Using stakeholders’ feedback to inform necessary improvements and adjustments to technology.
Focusing on technology improvements that will improve competitive positioning of the CrowdStrike products.
Providing recommendations for continuous improvement.

What You'll Need

Deep technical and operations skills in understanding the capabilities (strengths and weaknesses) of competitor offerings.
Strong analytical and communication skills to allow translation of competitive differentiation points into contextually relevant talking points.
Demonstrate a deep and broad knowledge of security issues and trends and are able to articulate a high-level security strategy to both technical and non-technical audiences.
Working in a role such as or similar to Competitive Strategist, Strategic Consultant, Enterprise Security Architect.
Experience with/exposure to Endpoint Security, Cloud Security, SIEM/Log Management, Mobile Security, Identity Security, Incident Response as well as other cyber security domains.
Regional travel is expected on a limited basis.

Remote-first culture
Market leader in compensation and equity awards

Comprehensive and inclusive health benefits
Physical and mental wellness programs
Paid parental leave, including adoption 
A variety of professional development and mentorship opportunities
Offices with stocked kitchens when you need to fuel innovation and collaboration

Our approach to cultivating a diverse, equitable, and inclusive culture is rooted in listening, learning and collective action. By embracing the diversity of our people, we achieve our best work and fuel innovation - generating the best possible outcomes for our customers and the communities they serve.

These independently operated brands have been serving their respective guests, franchisees and communities for decades. Through its Restaurant Brands for Good framework, RBI is improving sustainable outcomes related to its food, the planet, and people and communities.

University degree in business, marketing, finance, or related field.
2-3 years of work experience in QSR, Retailer, CPG supplier, or related field.

Experience working with SQL code data and visualization software such as Tableau/PowerBI.
Advanced Excel and PowerPoint skills.

Essential Skills

You have strong critical-thinking and conceptual problem-solving skills. You can debate complex issues, ask the right questions, interpret data and synthesize learnings.
You have strong organizational skills and high attention to detail.
You’re resilient and thrive in a fast-paced, high-pressure environment working on multiple projects simultaneously, with a sense of urgency and thoughtfulness.
You are an effective communicator and comfortable working in cross-functional teams.
Entrepreneurial spirit

What will your typical day look like?

The role of Global People Analytics within Global Talent supports and/or leads projects as identified. The current portfolio is varied and changes often. The individual will identify data-driven insights for an executive audience, support experimental research for developing people analytics methodologies, and have experience conducting advanced data modeling and developing analytics solutions.

As part of the Global Talent team you will:

Manage the development and execution of advanced people analytics and data visualization in support of global, member firm or global business initiatives as needed, including strategic priorities
Support the design, development, and delivery of research experiments from planning, collecting, analyzing, and interpreting results
Develop compelling, logically structured, actionable data driven insights (including storytelling of research/analytics findings) for all audience levels, including Executives
Maintain and coordinate data collection, transfer, storage, analysis, and retention processes
Support the governance, execution, and coordination of data-driven strategic projects, analyses, and visualizations for Global Talent, and liaise with Deloitte Technology and Global Finance
Assist with preparation of deliverables (e.g., meeting agendas, presentations, summary/notes, etc.) for key project meetings (e.g. Deloitte People Analytics community) or Global Talent meetings (e.g., Executive Leadership Team) and leadership communications
Support management of ongoing relationship with key stakeholders associated with project and priorities
Collaborate on the development of tools and technology to support people analytics and the application of behavioral science
Support knowledge sharing across member firms and global businesses, including the delivery of special initiatives (e.g., working groups with MF stakeholders, developing internal points of view on talent topics, timely support on global issues like COVID-19)
Stay informed on new research and techniques related to people/HR analytics that could be applied to Global Talent priority areas
Future responsibilities could shift to other projects. If so, the underlying responsibilities would be similar, yet the topic area would change.

Field Competitive Intelligence Analyst, Americas (Remote CT/MT) 

About The Role

As a Field Competitive Intelligence Analyst, you will support the CrowdStrike Sales and Executive Teams. You will work and support the CTO Labs and Field CTO Teams team at CrowdStrike. The Field CI team’s mission is to identify & deliver key competitive differentiators to support the international growth of customers, new markets, and TAM. This includes driving strategy through cross functional collaboration across the company including Product, Sales, Marketing, and more.

As the Field CI Analyst, you will be responsible for creating and communicating the company’s competitive differentiation strategy on a regional basis and working closely with the company’s product CTO’s, Product Managers and Field functions on a regular basis. You will also work closely with other groups within CrowdStrike, which includes: marketing, value management, legal and corporate affairs teams.

This role reports to the Manager, Competitive Intelligence Strategy. With your extensive cybersecurity background and your ability to think and operate at a strategic level, you will drive CrowdStrike’s technical vision and strategy and support on strategic engagements across the CrowdStrike organization.

What You'll Do

Support current customers and new customers by sharing CrowdStrike’s key competitive value differentiators, supporting the positioning of CrowdStrike as the leading thought leader for Cybersecurity with customers, partners, and analysts.
Driving and communicating CrowdStrike’s technology strategy to customers and partners as well as industry events.
Maintaining an in-depth knowledge of the cyber security industry, the competitive landscape and related industry developments to ensure we continue to be thought leaders who innovate ahead of the market.
Using stakeholders’ feedback to inform necessary improvements and adjustments to technology.
Focusing on technology improvements that will improve competitive positioning of the CrowdStrike products.
Providing recommendations for continuous improvement.

What You'll Need

Deep technical and operations skills in understanding the capabilities (strengths and weaknesses) of competitor offerings.
Strong analytical and communication skills to allow translation of competitive differentiation points into contextually relevant talking points.
Demonstrate a deep and broad knowledge of security issues and trends and are able to articulate a high-level security strategy to both technical and non-technical audiences.
Working in a role such as or similar to Competitive Strategist, Strategic Consultant, Enterprise Security Architect.
Experience with/exposure to Endpoint Security, Cloud Security, SIEM/Log Management, Mobile Security, Identity Security, Incident Response as well as other cyber security domains.
Regional travel is expected on a limited basis.

Job Summary

Closing Date: March 1, 2024

The Analyst, Data & Information, reporting to the Manager, Asset Development – Schaft Creek, will support GIS and data management on Schaft Creek Project. The position is based in Vancouver, Canada.

The candidate should be proficient with industry leading database and GIS applications, have a solid understanding of information and file management procedures and guidelines, and will facilitate continuous improvement and innovations in acquisition, storage, management, access, integration, and analysis of a wide range of spatial and time series data. The candidate should have a general understanding of Geoscience and Environmental Data Management. A demonstrable ability to collaborate with and contribute to strong multidisciplinary teams is crucial, as well as maintaining good relationships across similar disciplines within and outside of Teck.

Responsibilities

Be a courageous safety leader, adhere to and sponsor safety and environmental standards
Provide technical support and training for end-users of GIS software, including production of technical instructional guides and manuals, delivering training material and documenting workflows as require
Act as an administrator in Teck’s ArcGIS Online system, maintaining data/metadata standards and naming conventions, production and maintenance of web maps and web applications. Maintaining system and database health, license allocation and addressing issues as they arise
Support design and implementation of data management and integration workflows, queries, automated on-line technical and business reporting, and other methods of providing content to users in a balanced and scalable manner from multiple data types and sources including a variety of technical data, information and content types including: GIS, IoT sensors, maps, geologic sections, photos/videos, vector models, remote sensing data, satellite imagery, environmental and social baseline, virtual reality, documents and relevant administrative and commercial data etc
Collaborate with office, field and operations-based employees to understand business objectives and to provide guidance and advice for the efficient, appropriate and cost-effective management of project information throughout its lifecycle
Support implementation of new data capture tools as appropriate maximizing mobile and cloud solutions where possible and appropriate to facilitate real-time coordinated data driven decision making
Perform quality assurance on generated results to carry out data integrity and ensure metadata and spatial data standards are maintained
Administer enterprise database systems for drilling and sampling (acQuire), spatial GIS content (ESRI), 3D modelling (Leapfrog Central) and other related content (SharePoint, etc) where applicable
Assist with design and implementation of automated workflows, on-line technical and business reporting as required via the use of enterprise business intelligence tools
Support the development of O365 standards and best practices to ensure effective and appropriate use of tools
Understand how to set goals and prioritize tasks in order to achieve business results
Seek out and advises on trends in new technologies and best practices in GIS data management and makes recommendations on value added spatial initiatives

Build a culture of teamwork across all constituents and stakeholders and encourages cooperation and open communication
Foster a culture of open communication, focuses on building relationships across the organization and with external and internal partners, and invest in developing talent within the organization by providing recognition, challenge and mentorship

Experience developing custom apps and tools including roll-out, education and sustainment planning

About the job
Everest Clinical Research (“Everest”) is a full-service contract research organization (CRO) providing a broad range of expertise-based clinical research services to worldwide pharmaceutical, biotechnology, and medical device industries. We serve some of the best-known companies and work with many of the most advanced drugs, biologics, and medical devices in development today.

Everest has been an independent CRO since 2004 with a strong foundation as a statistical and data management center of excellence. Building on this foundation, Everest has successfully developed and established itself as a full-service CRO. Everest’s headquarters are located in Markham (Greater Toronto Area), Ontario, Canada with additional sites in Bridgewater (Greater New York City Area), New Jersey, USA, and Shanghai (Pudong Zhangjiang New District), China.

Everest is known in the industry for its high quality deliverables, superior customer service, and flexibility in meeting clients’ needs. A dynamic organization with an entrepreneurial origin, Everest continues to experience exceptional growth and great success.

Quality is our backbone, customer-focus is our tradition, flexibility is our strength…that’s us…that’s Everest.

To drive continued success in this exciting clinical research field, we are seeking committed, skilled, and customer-focused individuals to join our winning team as Biostatisticians for our Toronto/Markham, Ontario, Canada on-site location, or remotely from a home-based office anywhere in Canada in accordance with our Work from Home policy.

Key Accountabilities

 Leadership and Project Management:

Participate and/or lead efforts in resolving day-to-day work-related issues and problems, securing quality, and improving efficiency and productivity of statistical and programming operations.
Assist the Lead Biostatistician and/or Lead Programmer on assigned projects by applying project management skills and statistical and programming techniques; achieve quality and on‑time delivery of deliverables and earn client’s trust and repeat business.
Assist the Lead Biostatistician and/or Lead Programmer for a developmental program with more than one or two trials, coordinating with other Biostatisticians and Programmers, as well as project/program overall management personnel, to achieve program objectives.

Statistical Planning And Methodologies

Under supervision, provide statistical expertise for design, analysis, and reporting of clinical trials and research projects.
Write statistical sections of study protocols, perform sample size calculation, develop randomization specifications, and generate randomization codes.
Write Statistical Analysis Plans (SAPs) and properly address quality control (QC) review comments.
Create and maintain Statistical and Programming QC and Quality Assurance Plans for assigned projects or programs.
Provide input to unblinded data management plan when required.
Participate in research and development of statistical methodologies and processes.

Statistical Programming

Develop and/or review SDTM and ADaM dataset specifications.
Perform statistical programming to either build analysis datasets and generate statistical tables, listings, and graphs (TLGs) or perform QC validation of these datasets and TLGs.
Participate in statistical dry runs and final run by actively participating or contributing to project and resources management, addressing statistical and programming questions and interacting with data management to follow-up and resolve data issues.
Develop SDTM Study Data Reviewer’s Guide, discuss and incorporate Data Standards Reviewer’s review comments to ensure quality of the document.
Develop ADaM Analysis Data Reviewer’s Guide, discuss and incorporate Data Standards Reviewer’s review comments to ensure quality of the document.

Statistical Analysis And Reporting, Publication Support

Perform statistical modeling and analyses, implement new statistical analysis methods and strategies.
Perform statistical analysis as per SAP, and address peer/QC review comments and findings.
Perform statistical validation of study results, address additional QC validation comments and findings on the results.
Plan and conduct or contribute to the trial results reporting/dissemination meetings.
Contribute to the contents describing any deviation from the planned analysis and deviation from study conduct for the Clinical Study Report (CSR). Review CSR to ensure accuracy, completeness, and appropriateness of the interpretation of the statistical results.
Write statistical report or statistical sections of the CSR or perform peer review of the contents.
Perform statistical analyses for publications, including but not limited to abstracts, manuscripts, presentations, and posters.

Supporting Clinical Data Collection And Cleaning 

Provide statistical input to Case Report Forms (CRF) design and database/variable structure.
Provide statistical input to non-CRF data collection and acquisition methods and approaches.
Review Data Management Plan sections relating to critical data collection and cleaning. Provide statistical input to Data Validation Specification.
Specify and/or program database quality acceptance checks, assess and report data quality issues, and follow through until resolution.
Perform ongoing assessment and communication of data quality issues, including protocol deviations.
Assist data management and trial management team in preparing for database lock.
Perform Assigned QC Tasks to Ensure High Quality and Timely IWRS Services (Interactive Web-Based Response System, a Randomization and Drug Supply Management System):
These QC tasks include, but are not limited to, the following: QC review of the IWRS user requirement documents and user acceptance test (UAT) plans and results, participate in the UAT processes, and ongoing monitoring of the IWRS applications.
Complete job-required and project-specific training. Comply with applicable Everest and trial Sponsor’s Policies, Standard Operating Procedures, and Working Instructions.

Properly archive study files in accordance with trial Sponsor’s requirements.

Plan and carry out professional development activities.

For new Biostatisticians to the company, SAS training in the local programming environment will be provided by the internal SAS programmers. Intensive SAS programming for statistical analysis and the generation of statistical TLGs will be a requirement for the first year on the job. Hands on key data management activities such as participation in the writing of Data Management Plans, reviewing of data queries, and cleaning up databases, will also be a requirement for the first year on the job.

Qualifications And Experience

A Ph.D. degree in statistical science, mathematical analysis or related fields

OR

A Master’s degree plus at least 2 years highly relevant experience, with demonstrated ability and sustained performance.

Renseignements généraux

Vous avez envie d’action ? De travailler au sein d’une équipe dynamique ? De participer à l’amélioration de la qualité de vie des Québécoises et des Québécois ? Saisissez cette occasion de mettre de l’avant votre implication et votre créativité afin de faire concrètement la différence. Grâce à l’approche Entreprise en santé, le Ministère est soucieux de la qualité de vie au travail de son personnel et désire offrir un milieu collaboratif, mobilisateur et respectueux, qui favorise la santé et le mieux-être des personnes. Laissez-vous transporter vers de nouveaux défis et joignez-vous au ministère des Transports et de la Mobilité durable !

Rejoignez-nous aujourd’hui et faites partie d’une équipe passionnée qui écrira une nouvelle page de l’ère numérique!

 Analyste des données 

 Direction générale : Direction générale des ressources informationnelles et de la transformation numérique (DGRITN) 
 Direction générale adjointe : Direction générale adjointe de la gouvernance, de la sécurité informationnelle et de l’intelligence artificielle 
 Direction : Direction de la gouvernance des données et de l’intelligence artificielle (DGDIA) 
 Nombre d’emplois à pourvoir : 1 
 Statut de l’emploi : Régulier 
 Lieu de travail : 900 boulevard René-Lévesque Est, Québec* 
 Télétravail : en mode hybride 
 Horaire de travail : 35 heures par semaine 
 Date prévue d’entrée en fonction : Février 2024 
Étant un ministère qui œuvre partout sur le territoire et considérant la situation actuelle, nous avons l’opportunité de pourvoir cet emploi dans n’importe quelle région où il se trouve un bureau du ministère des Transports et la Mobilité durable

 Les défis que nous vous proposons 

La DGDIA est une toute nouvelle direction qui a la responsabilité de coordonner la gouvernance et la valorisation des données pour le Ministère et d’assurer le développement de l’automatisation et de l’intelligence artificielle aux différents secteurs d’affaires. Chez nous, vous trouverez un environnement de travail stimulant, des possibilités d’apprentissage en continu, une culture organisationnelle axée sur l’excellence et un climat de travail des plus agréables. Votre prochaine grande aventure professionnelle commence ici! En tant qu’analyste des données, vous serez responsable de la collecte, de l’analyse et de l’interprétation des données dans le contexte de projets d’intelligence artificielle. Dans votre rôle, vous aurez à :

 Analyser les besoins, les préoccupations, les enjeux et les problématiques de la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Définir, concevoir et mettre en place des mesures et des indicateurs liés à la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Tenir des registres précis des activités liées aux données, des méthodes utilisées et des résultats obtenus afin de garantir la reproductibilité et la transparence des travaux ; 
 Participer au choix des caractéristiques et variables les plus pertinentes à inclure dans les modèles afin d’améliorer les performances de l’intelligence artificielle ; 
 Promouvoir les bonnes pratiques, les normes et les standards au sein des solutions d’intelligence artificielle pour répondre au besoin de visualisation et de présentation de l’information ; 
 Garantir la qualité des résultats obtenus et contribuer à la certification des produits informationnels en soutenant la standardisation des méthodes d’exploitation des données ; 
 Assurer le lien de la gestion des données entre les secteurs d’affaires et les RI ; 
 Participer, en collaboration avec les ressources informationnelles, à la création des produits informationnels afin de permettre une utilisation conviviale et documenter les portées de ceux-ci. 

 Les avantages de travailler au ministère des Transports et de la Mobilité durable

 Apprends-en davantage sur nous : 

 FAIRE CARRIÈRE AU MINISTÈRE DES TRANSPORTS ET DE LA MOBILITÉ DURABLE 

Les défis à relever sont nombreux et stimulants. Intervenant de premier plan dans l’économie du Québec, le Ministère a pour mission et mandat d’assurer, sur l’ensemble de son territoire, la mobilité durable des personnes et des marchandises par des systèmes de transport efficaces et sécuritaires. Vaste organisation, le Ministère emploie plus de 8 500 personnes et gère 31 000 kilomètres de routes et 11 000 structures. Concrètement, le Ministère entretient, rend sécuritaires, conçoit et bâtit les vastes réseaux de transport maritime, ferroviaire, aérien et routier du Québec tout en innovant et en respectant l’environnement.

 LA DIRECTION DE LA GOUVERNANCE DES DONNÉES ET DE L’INTELLIGENCE ARTIFICIELLE (DVGDIA) 

La DGDIA conseille la haute direction et les utilisateurs sur l’utilisation optimale des données et des technologies d’IA. Son mandat est de développer, améliorer, entretenir et exploiter les technologies de l’information liées aux données et à l’IA pour soutenir la mission du Ministère et répondre à ses besoins. La direction élabore et promeut des normes, politiques et directives pour l’automatisation et l’utilisation responsable de l’IA, veillant à l’intégrité et à la sécurité des données. Elle encourage l’innovation en promouvant l’adoption de nouvelles technologies et en favorisant l’échange d’idées. Elle assure un rôle de surveillance pour s’assurer que l’utilisation des données et de l’IA respecte les lois et politiques en vigueur, établissant des mécanismes de contrôle et de vérification.

About the job
Marketing Statement

As the largest operating company in the integrated TransLink enterprise, Coast Mountain Bus Company (CMBC) operates a fleet of clean-fuel conventional and community shuttle buses, zero-emission trolley buses, and passenger ferry SeaBuses in Metro Vancouver, the largest single transit service area in Canada.

At CMBC, one of BC’s Top Employers, we're committed to providing an innovative, healthy, and engaging workforce. This is reflected in our workforce of over 5,500 employees performing over 400 unique jobs, who are committed and empowered to deliver service that attracts nearly 1.1 million passengers daily and connects people, businesses, and communities in the Metro Vancouver region.

We have the important job of helping our passengers get to work, appointments, visiting with family and friends, and back again every day. Metro Vancouver relies on us, and we take that as a point of pride.


Responsibilities

GENERAL ACCOUNTABILITY:

Represents the Asset Management Team in facilitating technical support and expertise in Enterprise Asset Management (EAM) applications and data analysis as it applies to Infrastructure Maintenance assets.

Work with departments to identify requirements, gather information, propose, and implement new procedures, applications, enhancements, system configuration changes, and liaise with BTS to ensure standards and procedures comply within company policy.

Coordinates with external support teams to ensure Asset Management and EAM organizational systems are functioning in accordance with business needs and requirements.

Provides guidance, expertise, and recommendations to various asset management stakeholders in CMBC and TransLink on various reporting systems, analytical tools, processes, and requirements to ensure information availability, quality, integrity, and reliability is maintained.

Conducts complex analysis, forecasting, reporting and documentation to improve effectiveness and to support continuous improvement of the Enterprise Asset Management systems for the division.

Provides training to various stakeholders on EAM reporting systems, analytical tools, processes, and requirements.

About the job
Chez RONA, plus de 26 000 employé(e)s cultivent leur passion chaque jour. Nos équipes sont animées par la volonté d’aider nos clients à faire de leurs projets une réalité, et engagées à faire une différence dans les communautés où nous sommes établis.

Nous exploitons ou desservons quelque 450 magasins corporatifs et marchands affiliés indépendants. Grâce à une offre de produits et services unique et à des formats complémentaires allant des quincailleries de quartier aux magasins de grande surface, nos enseignes RONA, Lowe’s, Réno-Dépôt et Dick’s Lumber sont outillées pour répondre à tous les besoins des rénovateurs amateurs, des rénovateurs expérimentés et des professionnels de la construction.

Vous avez le talent? Nous avons les outils! Chez nous, votre travail et vos idées contribuent à bâtir une organisation florissante. Votre voix sera toujours entendue et valorisée. Vous trouverez des possibilités de carrière à la mesure de vos ambitions et pourrez développer encore davantage l’ensemble de compétences qui vous rend unique.

Si vous cherchez à faire ce que vous aimez, nous pourrions être parfaits l’un pour l’autre.

Nos attentes :

Relevant de la Cheffe, Performance et analytique - Chaîne d’approvisionnement, l’Analyste, Science des Données - Chaîne d'approvisionnement, joue un rôle essentiel pour aider l’équipe d’optimisation de la Chaîne d’approvisionnement dans son mandat visant à favoriser l’excellence opérationnelle et l’amélioration continue de la performance dans toutes les fonctions de la chaîne d’approvisionnement. La personne choisie sera responsable de fournir aux membres de la haute direction les outils nécessaires pour prendre des décisions éclairées en ce qui concerne les opérations de la chaîne d’approvisionnement. Elle devra contribuer au développement et à la maintenance d’outils de veille économique et à la création de tableaux de bord IRC pour diverses équipes de la chaîne d’approvisionnement, en plus d’utiliser son expertise technique en matière de flux de données et de divers ensembles de données.

Ce poste exige de solides compétences en matière de veille économique, de connaissances techniques et analytiques, ainsi qu’une capacité d’adaptation permettant de s’épanouir dans un environnement de chaîne d’approvisionnement en constante évolution.

Le rôle :

Générer et fournir des rapports complets et précis et créer des tableaux de bord visuellement attrayants à l’aide d’outils de veille économique (p.ex., Power BI)
Concevoir et mettre en œuvre des modèles de données qui répondent aux besoins de l’entreprise, en garantissant l’intégrité des données et en optimisant les structures pour assurer l’efficacité des interrogations et des rapports
Collaborer avec les leaders de l’entreprise et les équipes interfonctionnelles pour comprendre les besoins en matière de veille économique
Démontrer une maîtrise de SQL, de l’entreposage de données et des processus ETL
Élaborer et mettre en œuvre la stratégie de veille économique de l’organisation en fonction des objectifs de l’entreprise
Procéder à une analyse approfondie des données afin d’obtenir des informations exploitables pour une prise de décision éclairée
Traduire les besoins d’affaires en spécifications techniques pour des solutions de veille économique efficaces
Déterminer de manière proactive les occasions d’amélioration et d’optimisation des processus
Assurer le leadership dans le domaine de la veille économique, en offrant des conseils aux analystes débutant(e)s et aux membres de l’équipe
Agir en tant qu’expert(e) en la matière pour les projets de veille économique, en apportant expertise et conseils
Favoriser une culture de prise de décision fondée sur les données au sein de l’organisation

Les compétences que nous recherchons :

Baccalauréat en ingénierie, en informatique ou dans un domaine connexe
Au moins 5 années d’expérience dans la préparation des données, l’entreposage des données et les bases de données
Au moins 5 années d’expérience avec MS Power BI, MicroStrategy ou des plateformes de veille économique et d’analyse comparables
Connaissance avancée de SQL (connaissance de Python un atout)
Maîtrise de la suite Microsoft Office 365, y compris des fonctionnalités avancées d’Excel (tableaux croisés dynamiques, Power Query)
Connaissance avancée de Microsoft Access (tables, requêtes, macros) et connaissance intermédiaire des bases de données telles que SQL Server et Oracle
Capacité de gérer et de manipuler des ensembles de données, en veillant à l’intégrité des données
Expérience de l’exploration de données à partir de systèmes multiples, de la manipulation d’ensembles de données externes et internes
Expérience dans le domaine de la chaîne d’approvisionnement, du transport ou de la distribution (un atout)
Pensée critique et compétences en matière de résolution de problèmes
Expérience dans un contexte de changement transformationnel et capacité d’adaptation aux besoins de l’entreprise
Capacité avérée d’assurer le leadership et le mentorat, en particulier en guidant les analystes débutant(e)s
Antécédents éprouvés d’exécution de tâches de façon efficace, à temps et sous pression, ainsi que de gestion efficace des priorités dans un environnement qui évolue rapidement

En travaillant chez RONA, vous bénéficierez de nombreux avantages, tels que ce qui suit :

Un centre de conditionnement physique, des activités sportives et des douches
Un centre de la petite enfance pouvant accueillir 78 enfants
Une cafétéria avec un menu de qualité cuisiné par un chef dédié, des options santé et des stations de café Brûleries FARO et Tim Hortons
Des rabais exclusifs aux employé(e)s, en plus d’un rabais de 10 % en magasin (dans toutes les enseignes de RONA)
Des avantages sociaux : assurances collectives, régime de retraite, primes annuelles, programme d’encouragement aux études, etc.
Des bornes de recharge pour voitures électriques
La possibilité d’évoluer au sein de l’organisation
Un environnement de travail inclusif et sécuritaire
Une sensibilité à l’équilibre travail-vie personnelle
Un employeur engagé dans sa communauté
Et plus encore!

Le générique masculin est utilisé sans discrimination et uniquement dans le but d’alléger le texte. RONA est déterminée à encourager la diversité et l’inclusion. About the job
About Agoda

Agoda is an online travel booking platform for accommodations, flights, and more. We build and deploy cutting-edge technology that connects travelers with more than 3.6 million accommodations globally. Based in Asia and part of Booking Holdings, our 6,000+ employees representing 90+ nationalities foster a work environment rich in diversity, creativity, and collaboration. We innovate through a culture of experimentation and ownership, enhancing the ability for our customers to experience the world.

THIS ROLE IS BASED IN BANGKOK, THAILAND (WITH RELOCATION PROVIDED)

Location: Bangkok, Thailand (*Not open for remote work.)

Get to Know our Team:

As part of the Supply Analytics, you will be responsible for identifying new partners and opportunities, cultivating a relationship with them, and working together with them to deliver the best outcome for our end customers. You would also be responsible with managing the day-to-day interaction with the partner and working closely with other teams within Agoda to ensure the partners needs are met.

We design tailored business and product solutions with our partners and help them generate measurable value. Members of our team are empowered and supported to grow their market(s) or accounts. We develop win-win relationships and leverage Agoda’s unique accommodations portfolio and tech solutions to bring our partners the advantages they seek. Utilizing our strong brand and resources, we build new channels to increase the visibility of Agoda, introduce more travelers to our great products and service and deliver significant revenues to the overall business.

The Opportunity: 

As an Analyst/Senior Analyst, you will report directly to either the Senior Manager or Associate Director within the Supply Department and this will be an individual contributor role. You will be responsible and fully empowered to work with the partners on the ground. You will be supported by a team within the Supply department and work closely with other Team members within Agoda.

In this Role, you’ll get to:

Translate internal briefs into analytical projects (to include refining the initial brief and asking the ‘right questions’, working through potential hypotheses and storyboarding the output)
Use and analyze data from multiple large-scale data warehouses and present statistically strong analysis to a wide range of business stakeholders
Proactively identify opportunities for growth within supply and the wider business
Drive new analytical initiatives and projects aimed at improving organizational efficiency and shaping Agoda supply
Identify, support, and lead projects aimed at scaling up the way the Supply organization leverages on data, insights, and intelligence
Automate manual operational processes and present back on time savings gained through modernization of business operations

What you’ll Need to Succeed:

At least 3-5+ years of experience working as an Analyst with experience in analytics/data science/insights/strategy/BI
Advanced working knowledge and hands-on experience in SQL
Strong knowledge and hands-on experience in data visualization tools such as Tableau (preferably) 
Expert domain of data analysis and data visualization tools and software such as Excel, Python (or R)
Bachelor’s degree ideally in a business or quantitative subject (e.g. computer science, mathematics, engineering, science, economics or finance)
A good understanding of statistical modelling knowledge or any machine learning technique knowledge (such as hypothesis testing, regression, logistic regression, random forest, etc.)
Good stakeholder management experience. Comfortable presenting to senior leadership and C-suite
Experience in conducting A/B testing experimentation
Strong experience in finding data insights and provide business recommendation to the business
A hacker’s mindset – the ability to build simple but clever and elegant solutions to new problems within significant resource, operational and time constraints through deep understanding of the business, creative problem solving, and a wide range of expertise in data, analytics, automation, programming, and prototyping
Excellent communicator with superior written, verbal, presentation and interpersonal communication skills
Data driven in both decision making and performance measurement
Extreme comfort in ambiguous, fast-paced environment
Ability to multi-task, prioritize and coordinate resources

It’s Great if you Have: 

MBA or Masters in a quantitative subject (e.g. computer science, mathematics, engineering, science, economics or finance)
Program management certifications (e.g. PMI, PRINCE2) to compliment your program management experience
Asian market experience
Travel industry / e-commerce / tech / consulting experience

About the job
Summary

Company Description

Assent is the leading solution for supply chain sustainability tailored for the world’s top-tier, sustainability-driven manufacturers. Hidden risks riddle supply chains, many of which weren't built with sustainability in mind. That's where we step in. With insights from experts, Assent is the tool manufacturers trust for comprehensive sustainability.

We've grown from $5 million to $85 million ARR in just six years. With our recent $350 million funding led by Vista Equity Partners, we're poised for even greater expansion and are on the lookout for outstanding team members.

Being a Certified B Corporation, we don't just advocate for sustainability – we live it. This certification underscores our commitment to environmental, social, and governance excellence. At Assent, your work will directly amplify transparency, sustainability, and fair practices worldwide.

Hybrid Work Model

At Assent, we proudly embrace a remote-first work model, valuing the flexibility and autonomy it provides our team. We also acknowledge the intangible benefits of occasional in-person workdays. For team members situated within 50 kms/31 miles of our five global offices in Ottawa, Eldoret, Penang, Columbus, and Amsterdam, you can expect to come into the office one day a week. Similarly, those near our co-working spaces in Nairobi and Toronto are encouraged to work onsite once a month.

Job Description

Assent is hiring a Senior Data Analyst for our Revenue Operations team. In this role, you will play a crucial part in enhancing our Revenue Operations by leveraging your expertise in Business Intelligence, analytics, and statistical modeling. As the Revenue Operations Senior Data Analyst, you will be instrumental in improving processes based on business requirements and collaborating closely with key business teams.

Key Requirements & Responsibilities:

Collaborate with Revenue departments, utilizing data modeling and statistical expertise to address business inquiries.
Analyze activities across Customer Success, Professional Services, and Sales to enhance operational workflows.
Implement data governance best practices and system guardrails in partnership with the Data Governance Council.
Develop and deliver training on predictive models and dashboards for Revenue Leadership and Operations Analysts.
Serve as a Subject Matter Expert in multiple data sources related to revenue data.
Manage projects from scoping through closure, working collaboratively with the Core Data Team.
Collaborate with the Core Data team to enhance analytics capabilities, expand the data catalog, and ensure data quality.
Identify and address data gaps in business processes and revenue systems.
Support Revenue Operations leadership in automating key metrics in collaboration with the Core Data Team.
Track data trends, providing actionable insights that drive revenue optimization.
Act as a power user for Revenue Ops tools, ensuring consistent use across the Go-To Market team.
Deliver training on systems and processes, championing Rev Ops best practices.


Qualifications

We strongly value your talent, energy and passion. It will also be valuable to Assent if you have the following qualifications:

5+ years of experience in a related role with proven success in supporting data analytics solutions within an organization.
Experience in python or R programming strongly desired.
Familiarity with data management tools such as Excel, Sheets, and SQL Server.
Strong quantitative analysis, problem-solving, and project management skills
Excellent project management skills with the ability to communicate complex concepts effectively at all levels of the organization.
Outstanding analytical ability and problem-solving skills with the ability to interpret data compellingly.
Ability to collaborate effectively with business managers, demonstrating influencing and negotiation skills.
Highly adaptable, flexible, and thrives in a fast-paced, dynamic business environment.
Meticulous attention to detail and the ability to make sense of large data sets.


Additional Information

Life at Assent

Wellness: We believe that you and your family’s well being is important. As a result, we offer vacation time that increases with tenure, comprehensive benefits packages (details vary by country), life leave days and more.

Financial Benefits: It’s not all about the money – well, it’s a little about the money. We understand that financial health is important and we offer a competitive base salary, a corporate bonus program, retirement savings options and more.

Life at Assent: There is purpose beyond your work. We provide our team members with flexible work options, volunteer days and opportunities to get involved in corporate giving initiatives.

Lifelong Learning: At Assent, curiosity is not only valued but encouraged. You will receive professional development days that are available to you the day you start

At Assent, we are committed to growing and sustaining an environment where our team members feel included, valued, and heard. Our diversity and equal opportunity practices are guided and championed by our Diversity and Inclusion Working Group and our Employee Resource Groups (ERGs).

Our commitment to diversity, equity and inclusion includes recruiting and retaining team members from diverse backgrounds and experiences, and fostering a culture of belonging where all team members are included, treated with dignity and respect, promoted on their merits, and placed in positions to contribute to business success.

If you require assistance or accommodation throughout any part of the interview and selection process, please contact talent@assent.com and we will be happy to help.

About the job
About Agoda

Agoda is an online travel booking platform for accommodations, flights, and more. We build and deploy cutting-edge technology that connects travelers with more than 3.6 million accommodations globally. Based in Asia and part of Booking Holdings, our 6,000+ employees representing 90+ nationalities foster a work environment rich in diversity, creativity, and collaboration. We innovate through a culture of experimentation and ownership, enhancing the ability for our customers to experience the world.

Get to Know our Team: 

In Product, ideas come alive. The world is moving fast so our culture empowers ownership and minimal bureaucracy. That’s the environment that enables you to do what you think is right – and quickly. Product Operations is a large, multicultural team of diversely talented individuals that serve as the curators of Agoda’s content. We manage all the content our customers and partners see on each of our products. As a part of our team, you will take ownership of processes that are critical to multiple other teams across the business. We are driving property-level content to map inventories from 3 rd  party supplies which will enable our reach to span the globe. Content Operations is also keen on self-improvement and innovation. We run our own structured data and analyze it to make impactful decisions. With the support of state-of-the-art technology and an enriching work environment, we strengthen the bottom line and drive new business for Agoda. 

The Opportunity: 

As an Analyst/Senior Analyst, you will report directly to either the Senior Manager or Associate Director within the Product Department and this will be an individual contributor role. You will be responsible and fully empowered to work with the partners on the ground. You will be supported by a team within the Product department and work closely with other Team members within Agoda. You will be instrumental in ensuring there is consistency in data being used for reporting, identifying value-added data to help the business grow as well as using data to make strategic business decisions. You will be expected to dig into data to provide business insights, guide decision-making and offer valuable inputs to further grow our business model.

In this Role, you’ll get to:

Translate internal briefs into analytical projects (to include refining the initial brief and asking the ‘right questions’, working through potential hypotheses and storyboarding the output)
Use and analyze data from multiple large-scale data warehouses and present statistically strong analysis to a wide range of business stakeholders
Conducted an analysis of customer behavior and their path through the platform, guaranteeing that the conversion rates for each front-end page met the established benchmarks and continually pinpointed opportunities for enhancement
Partnered with the Product Design and User Research team to generate fresh data-driven projects, one of which involved the development of a Dashboard designed for more efficient monitoring of user behavior and the measurement of novel business metrics
Drive new analytical initiatives and projects aimed at improving organizational efficiency and shaping Agoda supply
Identify, support, and lead projects aimed at scaling up the way the Supply organization leverages on data, insights, and intelligence
Automate manual operational processes and present back on time savings gained through modernization of business operations

What you’ll Need to Succeed:

Bachelor’s degree or higher in Mathematics, Business, Economics, Data Science, Information Technology or similar field
Bachelor’s Degree or higher in computer sciences, engineering, mathematics, statistics, data science or a related degree program. Masters degree preferred
Advanced domain of data analysis and data visualization tools and software such as Excel, SQL, Tableau, Python or similar
Analytical mindset, with proven track record in using data to measure performance and make decisions
Excellent problem-solving skills including the ability to analyze and resolve complex problems using data
Ability to work under pressure in a fast-paced and rapidly changing environment
Excellent communication skills (both verbal and written), with proven ability to convey complex messages clearly and with conviction
Team player with strong interpersonal, relationship-building, and stakeholder management skills

About the job
Opentext - The Information Company

As the Information Company, our mission at OpenText is to create software solutions and deliver services that redefine the future of digital. Be part of a winning team that leads the way in Enterprise Information Management.

The Opportunity

OpenText is looking for a strong candidate to be part of a diverse team responsible for the technical solution delivery of the SuccessFactors (HR System of Record) Recruiting and Onboarding.

This individual will report to the Director, IT- HR & Comp, and be able to effectively interact with the business partners and technical and operational resources.

This candidate will be an integral part of information systems development and integration for the OpenText IT Enterprise Applications organization.

You Are Great At

The Lead Systems Analyst will have the following responsibilities:

Lead the project delivery keeping multiple projects on track for a company and ensuring they are completed on time and according to specifications.
Led the implementation of Onboarding 2.0 and Phenom.
Lead M&A mass onboarding of acquisition employees and entities, integrations with other legacy HR, financial, and payroll applications, etc.
Support M&A activity to accelerate the planning and consolidation of core capabilities and applications such as employee migration, payroll, and benefit harmonization. 
Participate and lead Blueprint and design workshops with Business and IT Solution Architect. 
Responsible for transitioning solutions from a project delivery to an operational model coordinating with the IT Ent Apps Operations Team Lead.
Evaluate new systems and coordinate with the Solution Architect to formulate detailed plans to add new systems to the existing core infrastructure.
Enforce enterprise IT policies, procedures, and compliance within the HR IT work structure.
Create and maintain supporting technical documents about the platform and process.

What It Takes

Required Technical and Professional Expertise

Bachelor’s degree or equivalent in relevant discipline
Minimum 8 years experience with the SuccessFactors RCM, RMK, ONB 1.0 and ONB 2.0
Certified in SuccessFactors RCM and ONB
Experience with full cycle (end-to-end) implementations of SuccessFactors Recruiting and Onboarding Module
Strong understanding of SuccessFactors Employee Central
Experience with Phenom is preferred.
Self-starter that can work effectively as part of a team or individual contributor.
Strong skills, including analytical thinking, problem-solving, and superior communication, presentation, and interpersonal skills.

OpenText's efforts to build an inclusive work environment go beyond simply complying with applicable laws. Our Employment Equity and Diversity Policy provides direction on maintaining a working environment that is inclusive of everyone, regardless of culture, national origin, race, color, gender, gender identification, sexual orientation, family status, age, veteran status, disability, religion, or other basis protected by applicable laws. The role of Global People Analytics within Global Talent supports and/or leads projects as identified. The current portfolio is varied and changes often. The individual will identify data-driven insights for an executive audience, support experimental research for developing people analytics methodologies, and have experience conducting advanced data modeling and developing analytics solutions.

As part of the Global Talent team you will:

Manage the development and execution of advanced people analytics and data visualization in support of global, member firm or global business initiatives as needed, including strategic priorities
Support the design, development, and delivery of research experiments from planning, collecting, analyzing, and interpreting results
Develop compelling, logically structured, actionable data driven insights (including storytelling of research/analytics findings) for all audience levels, including Executives
Maintain and coordinate data collection, transfer, storage, analysis, and retention processes
Support the governance, execution, and coordination of data-driven strategic projects, analyses, and visualizations for Global Talent, and liaise with Deloitte Technology and Global Finance
Assist with preparation of deliverables (e.g., meeting agendas, presentations, summary/notes, etc.) for key project meetings (e.g. Deloitte People Analytics community) or Global Talent meetings (e.g., Executive Leadership Team) and leadership communications
Support management of ongoing relationship with key stakeholders associated with project and priorities
Collaborate on the development of tools and technology to support people analytics and the application of behavioral science
Support knowledge sharing across member firms and global businesses, including the delivery of special initiatives (e.g., working groups with MF stakeholders, developing internal points of view on talent topics, timely support on global issues like COVID-19)
Stay informed on new research and techniques related to people/HR analytics that could be applied to Global Talent priority areas
Future responsibilities could shift to other projects. If so, the underlying responsibilities would be similar, yet the topic area would change.

The Senior Business Intelligence Analyst will be responsible for the following duties and obligations:

Responsibilities: 
· Improve and support operational effectiveness through developing metrics and reporting to assist in making data-driven decisions. 
· Build and maintain dashboards to help stakeholders easily understand the feature performance and the next growth opportunities.

· Be proactive in doing deep dive analysis to provide actionable insights and measure the impacts.
· Monitor daily performance against key metrics to identify opportunities and anomalies. 
· Constantly review current operational processes and be a strategic partner in making recommendations for improvements. 
· Design and analyze A/B experiments to evaluate the impact of changes. 
· Stay relevant on industry trends and work with the product teams to develop high impact features. 
· Help define and shape companies' business intelligence products and tools.

RÉSUMÉ DES FONCTIONS

Le mandat des Services de la circulation est de fournir tous les services relatifs à la circulation, à la sécurité routière, aux enquêtes sur la circulation et à la gestion de la circulation dans la ville d’Ottawa.

Le titulaire réalise des études sur le terrain standard en matière d’ingénierie de la circulation, comme des études de files d’attente, de retards, de temps de parcours, de comptages de volume. Il enquête sur les plaintes relatives au réglage des feux de circulation, et il aide à assurer la tenue à jour de la base technique des données de circulation utilisée par le Système de circulation intégrée de la Ville d’Ottawa.

About the job

Responsibilities

RISQ’s main mission is to contribute to develop SG Group (the Group) business and returns through the implementation of an efficient risk management process. The VIE will work for a team (RISQ/COO) in charge of Governance, Risk and Compliance (GRC) project, Regulatory projects, and Ad-hoc requests from the Risk Managers.

The VIE will assist with the Governance, Risk Management and Compliance (GRC) initiative and his/her mission will be focused around 4 areas:

 Data analysis and identification of trends and data improvements
 Data quality checks to identify data quality issues
 Find opportunities to use Machine Learning / Artificial Intelligence and build the proof of concept
 Data reporting through BI Tool such as PowerBI

The GRC initiative aims to harmonize and integrate all risks and controls processes across multiple departments (RISQ, IT Risk, Compliance, Finance, Legal, etc.). The GRC tool developed for the initiative is named RSA Archer and currently has 150+ modules used mainly in the America region. Occasionally, the VIE will also support Risk Managers on ad-hoc requests.

Data analysis

 Analyze Archer data to ensure consistency of referential data uses (i.e.: organizational, geography, legal entity) and feasibility of reporting requirements
 Escalate any data issues such as duplication of records, unreportable multi selects, invalid records, etc.
 Review impact analysis on referential or taxonomy changes
 Perform ad hoc checks to guarantee data integrity
 Clean and normalize the data

Data quality

 Gather data quality needs with various risk teams
 Develop automatic checks on data
 Perform regular and automatized checks to ensure that data quality in GRC tool is good. Checks will include completeness of information as well as simple data quality checks (i.e.: events reported within # days)

ML/AI

 Identify opportunity for Machine Learning / Artificial Intelligence
 Gather Business Requirements and needs from end users
 Develop Proof of Concept and perform demo to end users

Reporting support

 Develop reports/dashboards in BI tool (Power BI) as per reporting needs provided

Provide demo to end users and release to production environment

Required

 Profile required

We would like to draw your attention to the fact there that your VIE mission could potentially get postponed, depending on the evolution of the health crisis and subjects to the decision made by the Crisis and Support Centre of the Ministry of Europe and Foreign Affairs (MEAE). About the job
Everest Clinical Research (“Everest”) is a full-service contract research organization (CRO) providing a broad range of expertise-based clinical research services to worldwide pharmaceutical, biotechnology, and medical device industries. We serve some of the best-known companies and work with many of the most advanced drugs, biologics, and medical devices in development today.

Everest has been an independent CRO since 2004 with a strong foundation as a statistical and data management center of excellence. Building on this foundation, Everest has successfully developed and established itself as a full-service CRO. Everest’s headquarters are located in Markham (Greater Toronto Area), Ontario, Canada with additional sites in Bridgewater (Greater New York City Area), New Jersey, USA, Shanghai (Pudong Zhangjiang New District), China and Taipei, Taiwan.

Everest is known in the industry for its high quality deliverables, superior customer service, and flexibility in meeting clients’ needs. A dynamic organization with an entrepreneurial origin, Everest continues to experience exceptional growth and great success.

Quality is our backbone, customer-focus is our tradition, flexibility is our strength…that’s us…that’s Everest.

To drive continued success in this exciting clinical research field, we are seeking committed, skilled, and customer-focused individuals to join our winning team as Senior Biostatisticians for our Markham, Ontario on-site location, or remotely from a home-based office anywhere in Canada in accordance with our Work from Home policy.

Key Accountabilities

 Leadership and Project Management:
Lead efforts in resolving day to day work related issues and problems, securing quality, improving efficiency and productivity of statistical and programming operations.
Lead assigned projects by applying project management skills, statistical and programming techniques; achieve quality and on time delivery of deliverables, earn client’s trust and repeat business.
 Statistical Planning and Methodologies:
Provide statistical expertise for design, analysis and reporting of clinical trials and research projects.
Contribute to the writing of statistical sections of study protocols, perform sample size calculation, develop randomization specifications, and generate randomization codes.
Write Statistical Analysis Plans (SAPs) and properly address Peer Statistician review comments.
Create and maintain Statistical and Programming Quality Control (QC) and QA Plans for assigned projects.
Provide input to unblinded data management plan when required.
Assist in research and development of statistical methodologies and processes.
 Statistical Programming:
Develop and/or review ADaM dataset specifications. Review and provide input to SDTM dataset specifications when required.
Perform QC validation of analysis datasets and TLGs.
Perform third level review of dry runs and final run.
Lead statistical dry runs and final run by actively participating or contributing to project and resources management, addressing statistical and programming questions and interacting with data management to follow up and resolve data issues.
Review and provide input to the Analysis Data Reviewer’s Guide, discuss and incorporate Data Standards Reviewer’s review comments to ensure quality of the document.
 Statistical Analysis and Reporting, and Publication Support:
Perform statistical analysis as per SAP, and address peer/QC review comments and findings.
Perform statistical validation of core results, address additional QC validation comments and findings on the core results.
Plan and conduct or contribute to the trial results reporting/dissemination meetings.
Under supervision contribute to the contents describing any deviation from the planned analysis and deviation from study conduct for the Clinical Study Report (CSR). Review CSR to ensure accuracy, completeness and appropriateness of the interpretation of the statistical results.
Write statistical report or statistical sections of the CSR.
Perform statistical analyses for publications, including but not limited to abstracts, manuscripts, presentations and posters.
 Supporting Clinical Data Collection and Cleaning:
Provide statistical input to Case Report Forms (CRF) design and database/variable structure.
Provide statistical input to non-CRF data collection and acquisition methods and approaches.
Review Data Management Plan sections relating to critical data collection and cleaning. Provide statistical input to Data Validation Specification.
Specify and/or program database quality acceptance checks, assess and report data quality issues, and follow through until resolution.
Perform ongoing assessment and communication of data quality issues, including protocol deviations.
Assist data management and trial management team in preparing for database lock.
 Complete job required and project-specific training. Comply with applicable Everest and trial sponsor’s policies, SOPs, and work instructions.
 Properly archive study files in accordance with trial sponsor’s requirements.
 Plan and carry out professional development activities.

Qualifications And Experience

A Ph.D. degree in statistical science, mathematical analysis or related fields plus 2 years highly relevant experience or a Master’s degree plus 4 years highly relevant experience, with demonstrated ability and sustained performance.

About The Role

CrowdStrike Intelligence, a core component of CrowdStrike Counter Adversary Operations, is seeking to hire a Senior Intelligence Analyst for its Intelligence Analysis Cell (IAC) to focus on eCrime. This position will primarily conduct analysis on established and emerging actors in the eCrime ecosystem, criminal operating models, monetization techniques, and the geographic diversity of eCrime. This position is instrumental in providing unique insight into the strategic context and operating environment of adversaries through finished intelligence products used by CrowdStrike customers and stakeholders.

What You'll Do

Analyze financially-motivated cyber actors and compose long- and short-form finished intelligence reports related to actor tracking, monetization methods, commodity and closed malware groups, and fraud techniques
Research, assess, and report on specific cyber threat actor and adversary capabilities, motivations, and Tactics, Techniques, and Procedures (TTPs)
Provide clear and concise written responses to customer requests for information (RFIs) and contribute to briefings where necessary
Work in a collaborative environment with other analysts, technical experts, and customer-facing personnel
Assist in research prioritization efforts and intelligence gap identification

What You'll Need

5+ years’ experience conducting research in the field of eCrime to include producing intelligence assessments and handling ad-hoc requests for information (RFIs)
A strong understanding of current and emerging threats related to financially-motivated computer intrusions, scams, and fraud techniques
In-depth knowledge of current underground criminal forums and marketplaces, digital currency use in criminal activity, enabling infrastructures, monetization methods, money laundering, and access brokers
A general understanding of commonly used criminal malware, botnets, and access brokers
An ability to express complex technical and non-technical concepts verbally, graphically, and in writing
Excellent English writing and open-source research skills
Comprehensive practical knowledge of intelligence analysis and collection skills
An analytic mindset capable of applying best practices such as structured analysis, awareness of biases and other pitfalls, and critical thinking in source evaluation
Undergraduate degree in cybersecurity, general intelligence studies, security studies, criminal justice, political science, international relations; or equivalent military training and experience in a cyber intelligence/security MOS
Technical and non-technical security certifications pertaining to financial crimes analysis, anti-money laundering (AML), or cyber threat intelligence

Preferred

Graduate or professional degrees in any of the aforementioned fields
Ability to utilize graph analysis tools (e.g., i2 Analyst Notebook, Maltego) to create both working-level and presentation-grade visualization charts
Experience contributing to Computer Network Operations (CNO) campaign tracking, including working with technical indicators pertaining to malware and network infrastructure
Formal foreign language training or competency, especially in Russian, Farsi, Chinese, Spanish, or Portuguese

About the job
The Senior Biostatistician serves a lead role on projects. He/she interacts with team members in designing and analyzing clinical trials. Key responsibilities and skills include, but are not limited to:

Responsible for protocol development including study design, sample size estimation, randomization, and statistical analysis plan for assigned studies.
Provide statistical oversight to studies and assure adequate quality and consistency with project requirements.
Responsible for accuracy and completeness of database quality checks.
Responsible for assuring that data for statistical analyses are complete, accurate and consistent.
Responsible for statistical analysis plans and the accuracy and timeliness of statistical input into reports or decisions.
Responsible for validity of analysis and alternative analysis strategies when unforeseen circumstances arise.
Demonstrates extensive understanding of statistical concepts and methodologies. Recognizes and corrects flaws in scientific reasoning and statistical interpretation.
Responsible for accuracy and consistency of statistical tables, figures, and data listings, accuracy of report text, and consistency between summary tables in the body of reports and the corresponding source tables and listings.
Responsible for statistical methods section for the reports. Identifies and corrects flaws in interpretation of results, inconsistency in presentation or inference, adherence to the report guidelines, and assures project-wide consistency.
Effectively mentor non-statistical peers with regards to statistical methodology and provide appropriate background, motivation, and training to junior statisticians.
Effectively coordinate assignments and review deliverables so that projects are delivered on time with high quality.

 Analyste des données 

 Direction générale : Direction générale des ressources informationnelles et de la transformation numérique (DGRITN) 
 Direction générale adjointe : Direction générale adjointe de la gouvernance, de la sécurité informationnelle et de l’intelligence artificielle 
 Direction : Direction de la gouvernance des données et de l’intelligence artificielle (DGDIA) 
 Nombre d’emplois à pourvoir : 1 
 Statut de l’emploi : Régulier 
 Lieu de travail : 900 boulevard René-Lévesque Est, Québec* 
 Télétravail : en mode hybride 
 Horaire de travail : 35 heures par semaine 
 Date prévue d’entrée en fonction : Février 2024 
Étant un ministère qui œuvre partout sur le territoire et considérant la situation actuelle, nous avons l’opportunité de pourvoir cet emploi dans n’importe quelle région où il se trouve un bureau du ministère des Transports et la Mobilité durable

 Les défis que nous vous proposons 

La DGDIA est une toute nouvelle direction qui a la responsabilité de coordonner la gouvernance et la valorisation des données pour le Ministère et d’assurer le développement de l’automatisation et de l’intelligence artificielle aux différents secteurs d’affaires. Chez nous, vous trouverez un environnement de travail stimulant, des possibilités d’apprentissage en continu, une culture organisationnelle axée sur l’excellence et un climat de travail des plus agréables. Votre prochaine grande aventure professionnelle commence ici! En tant qu’analyste des données, vous serez responsable de la collecte, de l’analyse et de l’interprétation des données dans le contexte de projets d’intelligence artificielle. Dans votre rôle, vous aurez à :

 Analyser les besoins, les préoccupations, les enjeux et les problématiques de la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Définir, concevoir et mettre en place des mesures et des indicateurs liés à la gestion des données au Ministère ; 
 Tenir des registres précis des activités liées aux données, des méthodes utilisées et des résultats obtenus afin de garantir la reproductibilité et la transparence des travaux ; 
 Participer au choix des caractéristiques et variables les plus pertinentes à inclure dans les modèles afin d’améliorer les performances de l’intelligence artificielle ; 
 Promouvoir les bonnes pratiques, les normes et les standards au sein des solutions d’intelligence artificielle pour répondre au besoin de visualisation et de présentation de l’information ; 
 Garantir la qualité des résultats obtenus et contribuer à la certification des produits informationnels en soutenant la standardisation des méthodes d’exploitation des données ; 
 Assurer le lien de la gestion des données entre les secteurs d’affaires et les RI ; 
 Participer, en collaboration avec les ressources informationnelles, à la création des produits informationnels afin de permettre une utilisation conviviale et documenter les portées de ceux-ci. 

 Les avantages de travailler au ministère des Transports et de la Mobilité durable

 20 jours de vacances après seulement un an de service et 13 jours fériés ;

 Service de formation et de développement au sein de l’organisation ;

1- Pour être considérée, toute scolarité effectuée hors du Canada doit faire l’objet d’une évaluation comparative (attestation d’équivalence) délivrée par le ministère de l’Immigration, de la Francisation et de l’Intégration (MIFI).

2- Une personne en attente de la preuve de son statut de résident permanent ou d’un permis de travail peut soumettre sa candidature au présent processus de sélection. Toutefois, elle devra être autorisée à travailler légalement au Canada au moment de sa nomination.
